                   ฿ ฐฐ฿  r c n  ฐ   ฿ฐ฿ฐ
                 ฐ    ฿฿฿       ฿  ฿฿฿   ฿฿
       ฿฿฿       ฐ฿   ฿   ฿฿      ฐ    
 ฿   ฿ฐ ฐ  ฐ ฐ ฐฐ ฐฐ฿฿ ฐฐฐฐ ฐ ฐฐฐ
฿฿฿฿฿฿     ฿฿   ฐ฿฿       ฿ฐ   ฿ ฿฿฿
 ฿฿       ฿฿   ฐ  ฿   ฿฿฿฿    ฿  ฿      ฿ฐ฿
    ฿฿฿฿฿  ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿             ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿ฐ     ฿
                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Okay, I am writing this to bring out the truth about some shit I did  บ
 บ  like 5 months ago.  Brutus and I were running Legacy around January or    บ
 บ  February.  Entropy set us up with a guy named Waverider who said he had   บ
 บ  the game of the year and all the usual bull shit.  No problem.  He tells  บ
 บ  us he has the full Alpha version of the game and wants us to release it.  บ
 บ  Soo, we decided not to release the source and have a programmer work on   บ
 บ  it and make patches for things like modem play.  All was fine, Waverider  บ
 บ  promised no one else would get the source code, and everyone was happy;   บ
 บ  except Waverider. He couldn't understand that because he could supply     บ
 บ  only one release, he wasn't a full member.  That was just the Legacy      บ
 บ  policy at the time.  He was only supposed to get credit for that release  บ
 บ  and any patches that might proceed it, and this was worked out with him   บ
 บ  and Stormside (I think) from Motiv8.  M8 wanted to courier it.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So 2 days after we release this game, ROR releases the source code    บ
 บ  to it.  Kind of amazing seeing as no one was supposed to have it.  TKLP   บ
 บ  did some nice ass kissing (that is of course the job of every group       บ
 บ  leader) and got it.  I went to the Motiv8 leaders and talked to them      บ
 บ  about kicking him from M8 or punishing him in some way for breaking his   บ
 บ  word to another group, and M8's word along with it.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I tried for 2 days to get something done, they kept saying they       บ
 บ  would take some sort of disciplinary measure, but nothing was happening.  บ
 บ  As a result of this, I e-mailed the company that programmed this.  All I  บ
 บ  gave them was Waverider's IRC handle.  The next thing I knew, they were   บ
 บ  raiding his house.  Yes, I am a dick, but I thought it was funny.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few days later I got attacked by a ton of people that know nothing  บ
 บ  of what they were talking about.  It died a bit after that, but           บ
 บ  Waverider, in court, narqed saying that TKLP was the releaser of the      บ
 บ  source.  This is confirmed in Issue #16 of RCN by TKLP himself in an      บ
 บ  interview.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, 4 months later, I have assholes that think they know something   บ
 บ  starting shit, I have a lamer sending out fake logs saying all kinds of   บ
 บ  shit that was never said, and another magazine printed distorted facts.   บ
 บ  By the way, I like the other magazines, just one of their head people is  บ
 บ  jealous of RCN or something and wants to start shit.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So this is the story of what REALLY happened.  I have no reason to    บ
 บ  lie, this shit is old news, but some people have a hard time letting go   บ
 บ  of the past.  In short, we made a deal, he fucked me, I tried to resolve  บ
 บ  it on IRC with his leaders, they stalled, I took care of it.  It's a      บ
 บ  very simple thing, the scene has its limits, and those boundaries should  บ
 บ  not be crossed. I had a reason behind my telling Wave not to release the  บ
 บ  source.  I am a responsible person and I knew we would only release a     บ
 บ  compiled version, but they didn't think that way.  Releasing the source   บ
 บ  code of an ALPHA version of a program is like saying a fat "FUCK YOU" to  บ
 บ  the company, as this was uncopyrighted material.  Any Joe Blow could      บ
 บ  have taken that and copyrighted it.  It is one thing to release pirated   บ
 บ  software.  The company can write that off as a loss.  It's another        บ
 บ  thing, however, to release material that that company has spent           บ
 บ  countless hours on and ruin it all for them.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Oh, and in closing, if anyone thinks they can narq on me, I keep NO   บ
 บ  WAREZ at my house or on my system, I don't card, and I don't phreak.  So  บ
 บ  have fun trying! :-)                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  RoadRebel                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RoadRebel,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You've covered it all there.  Thanks for clearing things up.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is Defender Zeta of Rapier, Logistix, Alliance, and Mortality    บ
 บ  writing to let you know that I am retiring.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Im quitting the scene as of now.  As I've gone from a lamer with no   บ
 บ  clue to a lamer with a clue I've come to the decision that the scene has  บ
 บ  become a waste of time.  I have put in 7-10 hours a day after school for  บ
 บ  about 17 months now.  I'm totally burned out, my girlfriend dumped me     บ
 บ  <the bitch ;) >, and it seems that most of my friends are in the scene.   บ
 บ  I'm quitting becuase the scene isn't what i thought it would be.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's been fun and quite educational <I have no clue how to use half   บ
 บ  the illegal crap ive learned off other people online>.  The scene         บ
 บ  interferes with jobs, lifes, famlies, and is generally a waste of time.   บ
 บ  I thought it over.   If my biggest thrill is to get #1 on a board or a    บ
 บ  site i need a fucking life.  I've stayed awake for days at a time to      บ
 บ  increase my place in the scene.  I have made friends and enemies.  It's   บ
 บ  been an interesting experience.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I started out as a lamer with a 14.4 and no clue and now I'm leaving  บ
 บ  as a lamer with a 14.4 and no life.  The scene is addictive as hell.      บ
 บ  Don't even bother to deny it.  Almost every trader I know has said at     บ
 บ  some point or another 'I'm quitting..  this shit is messing up my life'.  บ
 บ  Most come back in a month or so...  I should know...  I've quit 5 times   บ
 บ  now..  and each time something happens to drag me back.  I'd like to      บ
 บ  take this occasion to tell lesser traders that as you get farther into    บ
 บ  the scene you will be dragged into alot of political crap.  It's          บ
 บ  annoying and it will take up about 80% of your time.  Finding out who's   บ
 บ  the shit and who's not takes up about 60% of your trading time and iRC    บ
 บ  itself take about 80% of your time.  I would encourage traders who are    บ
 บ  on the local scale and who havent gotten into the group scene yet to      บ
 บ  quit while your ahead..  just stay in #Exceed and rape the DCC lamers..   บ
 บ  its almost the best way to do it and stay independent.  I'd encourage     บ
 บ  most of the traders out there to quit now. The Feds will find a legal     บ
 บ  loop hole in our legal system that will allow them to trace you and       บ
 บ  arrest you.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Currently, the scene in the USA exists on its scale because the law   บ
 บ  cannot touch us.  We are invincible.  We are in vast numbers and our      บ
 บ  legions grow daily.  On the flip side we are ultra competitive, quite     บ
 บ  often have misplaced priorities which are focused on the scene.  The      บ
 บ  scene is a colossial waste of time.  In all my moving about gigs of crap  บ
 บ  I have only downloaded and unzipped about 12 games.  The scene is full    บ
 บ  of crap that no one bothers to leech and unzip.  It gets expensive after  บ
 บ  a while.  The scene starts out fun by pretending we are the best board    บ
 บ  traders on earth.  It ends with us being the best board and site traders  บ
 บ  on earth but with no life.  Fan Fan la Tulipe said it best when he said   บ
 บ  the entire scene was a dream and a fantasy.  It's based on the idea that  บ
 บ  one day you will become ELiTE enuff to have your name be known forever    บ
 บ  in the scene.  This is crap, if a person quits the scene he is forgotten  บ
 บ  in maybe 6 months to a year tops if he was a super trader.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Look at Captain Blood <not the CD Rom one..  the trader one>, he was  บ
 บ  the shit.  He was a major member of Razor, DOD, and a ton of other        บ
 บ  groups.  In one day (ONE) he was kicked off every major board and site    บ
 บ  and he was the object of ridicule and jokes.  Don't imagine that the      บ
 บ  scene itself gives a fuck about you.  You will make friends and they      บ
 บ  will miss you but they will make new friends and forget about you when    บ
 บ  your a hasbin.  The scene is impersonal and it doesnt care about you.     บ
 บ  Your friends will miss you but like I said..  in time they will forget    บ
 บ  about you.  My advice is to chill and get a girlfriend <or in             บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After reading your Issue #16, I decided to throw in my 2 cents on an  บ
 บ  issue that has been bothering me.  First of all, the issue of trading     บ
 บ  and talent.  Please let it be known that it takes NO talent whatsoever    บ
 บ  to be a courier.  People base respect and popularity on "talent."  It     บ
 บ  takes absolutely no talent whatsoever to sit and type on a keyboard for   บ
 บ  a few hours and move files.  It does, however, take knowhow and contacts  บ
 บ  to get the job doe right.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      People say that DCC couriers are lame and have no talent, but this    บ
 บ  is far from the truth.  The truth of the matter is that it takes no       บ
 บ  talent to do any bit of couriering or releasing.  If you think it does,   บ
 บ  then you're a fool. My little brother could do what any of you do, if I   บ
 บ  were to sit down and teach him how.  We all have special talent in        บ
 บ  certain areas of our life, but playing in the warez world is not one of   บ
 บ  them by any means.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      How fucking hard is it to sit there and DCC a file or download it     บ
 บ  off of a BBS and move it around?  Your average bum could do that, but     บ
 บ  yes, it does take time and contacts to be able to get that.  All that     บ
 บ  entails, however, is meeting the right people and moving the proper       บ
 บ  meggage.  Now most people will find this offensive but I don't give a     บ
 บ  shit.  The people in RiSC and Amnesia and Digital and fATE and all of     บ
 บ  them for that matter, the ones who people consider "gods of warez"        บ
 บ  really are no better than the guys in #warez5 or #lamewarez or whatever.  บ
 บ  They just have more time on their hands (which tells you what?  They      บ
 บ  have no outside life) because I can sit and move for hours and hours a    บ
 บ  day tons of megs of files and be considered a "talented kick-ass          บ
 บ  trader."  Meanwhile I have no real outside life, so that says in real     บ
 บ  life most of these so called "warez gods" are probably a bunch of         บ
 บ  weirdos with no friends or no girlfriend or job.  They can just sit       บ
 บ  around forever and move files, something you people need to think about   บ
 บ  next time you go kissing ass with the top courier or next time you call   บ
 บ  your average Joe Blow a lamer.  That lamer probably has a job and a       บ
 บ  girlfriend and friends and something real to do with his time!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now on to the next issue.  The word "lame" or "lamer."  I am so sick  บ
 บ  to death of this word.  It is so overused and over-rated.  When you deam  บ
 บ  someone lame you are deaming yourself better than them.  Again, that      บ
 บ  says in the scene that in order for you to deam someone lame, that you    บ
 บ  must be better than them.  How?  Well, by moving more files or releasing  บ
 บ  more stuff or sucking dick with bigger people (status-wise), but when     บ
 บ  you step back and come to reality, that lamer probably has a life and     บ
 บ  does more with his time than type on a keyboard, so now in retrospect     บ
 บ  who is lame?  The guy going to a bar with his friends or getting laid on  บ
 บ  Saturday night, or the guy who sits at home in front of his PC typing     บ
 บ  "mput *.zip" (wow, that takes LOTS of talent!).  None of you are better   บ
 บ  than anybody else.  None of you have any talent when it comes to warez,   บ
 บ  because it takes no talent.  So next time you go to call someone lame     บ
 บ  think about yourself and why you are doing that, but most of the people   บ
 บ  who do that are so wrapped up in the scene that they don't know the       บ
 บ  difference between reality and the scene, and THAT, my friend, is lame!   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Anonymous                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I've often tried to describe to my friends who are not educated in    บ
 บ  the ways of the elite just how the scene operates.  The best analogy I    บ
 บ  could ever come up with is one of a pyramid.  The best (and the few at    บ
 บ  the top), the semi-talented (a medium amount of these) in the middle,     บ
 บ  and the unskilled at the bottom (thousands of these).  The hardcore       บ
 บ  traders and top sites are probably at the top, mediocre groups in the     บ
 บ  middle, and DCC couriers/Anon Sites/#WarezX channels at the bottom.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Knowing this, we can accurately decide the DCC courier's place.       บ
 บ  When used in moderation, DCC-ing can be an effective and efficient way    บ
 บ  of moving files around.  Distributing group NFOs, applications, group     บ
 บ  taggers/dizzers.  DCC-ing is probably the best way to move some files to  บ
 บ  a large target audience.  FTP sites, however fast, can get bogged down    บ
 บ  with large amounts of people, but a DCC process can facilitate many       บ
 บ  people at the same time.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The reason why DCC couriers are regarded as "The epitome of the lame  บ
 บ  Pericles" is probably because it doesn't take much talent to offer        บ
 บ  something and set the /ptime to 10 mins or so.  There is little or no     บ
 บ  competition, no one can really tell who is the fastest, and the demanded  บ
 บ  software can be days to weeks old.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The reason people get into DCC trading can be anywhere from laziness  บ
 บ  to the "hands-on" feel of DCC couriering.  A friend of mine once told me  บ
 บ  that it was gratifying watching all the numbers to the processes go, and  บ
 บ  that when people would leech his files, they would thank him and it made  บ
 บ  the whole process worthwhile.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I can safely say that DCC couriering may be a fun and effective       บ
 บ  medium by which one can courier, if used in conjunction with FTP          บ
 บ  trading.  I myself have done both FTP and DCC couriering, and have mixed  บ
 บ  emotions of both worlds.  FTP is definitely more competitive, a lot of    บ
 บ  work, and at the same time very gratifying when you beat the shit out of  บ
 บ  someone.  DCC is something I don't think I'll ever do again, save         บ
 บ  offering the latest RCN when it comes out.  There is no more motivation   บ
 บ  for me to risk being caught by some FBI/Chris Carter person just to       บ
 บ  offer files to people I'll probably never know.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I believe that if you're at the top, or near the top, your files      บ
 บ  will make it to almost all the DCC traders there are out there.           บ
 บ  Therefore, the pyramid shape leads me to believe, in order to             บ
 บ  effectively affect the most amount of people, you must climb higher on    บ
 บ  it.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Anonymous                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First, I'd just like to say I've enjoyed your e-mag thus far.  It     บ
 บ  makes for some interesting reading to hear the thoughts of other people   บ
 บ  in the scene that I wouldn't hear otherwise.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In response to Tuxedo Mask's article on DVD-ROMs, I don't understand  บ
 บ  how he could conclude the advent of DVD technology could be good for the  บ
 บ  scene.  It's obvious that CD-ROM titles have hurt the warez scene.  More  บ
 บ  often than not, CD-RIPs don't work, aren't worth the time to download     บ
 บ  considering the enjoyment (for games) or usefulness (for utils)           บ
 บ  received, and have some critical feature of the program cut out for       บ
 บ  space reasons.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not to mention the fact that some titles simply are not released      บ
 บ  because of their size.  The reason for all of this is clear.  Mass        บ
 บ  storage technologies are increasing at an exponential rate, while data    บ
 บ  transmission technologies are increasing only geometrically.  In the      บ
 บ  last couple of years, we have seen the common communications tool double  บ
 บ  in speed (the modem from 14.4kbps to 28.8kbps), but the average game has  บ
 บ  increased by 500 to 800 percent.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I don't know how closely Tuxedo Mask follows technicial matters, but  บ
 บ  he neglected to mention that DVD-ROM technology allows not only for       บ
 บ  double sided media, but also for double layered media.  This is           บ
 บ  accomplished by having two rows of pits at different depths and           บ
 บ  switching the focus of the laser.  Using these techniques, data           บ
 บ  capacities could be quadrupled to 17 gigabyte.  Doubt software            บ
 บ  manufacturer's will find use for that much space?  Would you have         บ
 บ  believed when CD-ROMs first came out that software would not only fill    บ
 บ  them, but grow to the point where some (horridly bad) games ship on 10    บ
 บ  platters?                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Considering the damage that CD-ROMs have done thus far, and the       บ
 บ  plausible explosive popularity of the DVD-ROM format looming on the       บ
 บ  horizon (due in part because DVD-ROM will be introduced in parallel as    บ
 บ  the new video & audio storage standard), DVD-ROMs will most definitely    บ
 บ  hurt the scene.  I think the DVD-ROM issue raises some important          บ
 บ  questions on the future of the scenes "technological feasibility".        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Just my thoughts of course...                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Necromancer               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Necromancer,                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Tuxedo Mask was merely stating two possibilities of how the DVD-ROM   บ
 บ  could effect the scene.  He didn't fail to mention how the DVD-ROM could  บ
 บ  be the next scene "killer" finishing off the job that the CD-ROM          บ
 บ  started, but he might have over emphasized on how the DVD-ROM could help  บ
 บ  regular pirates.  He mentioned that a tool such as the upcoming DVD-ROM,  บ
 บ  all of which are recordable, would be a great asset to anyone who wishes  บ
 บ  to start their own warez library of games.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You mentioned that one DVD-ROM could potentially hold up to 17 gigs,  บ
 บ  however, that data is no longer up to date with the latest in news.  The  บ
 บ  latest estimates show that the original designers miscalculated the       บ
 บ  potentials of the DVD-ROM, and it seems more likely now, that the         บ
 บ  DVD-ROM will be only be one sided, due to production costs, and thus,     บ
 บ  will only be able to hold up approximately 4 gigs, and not 17 gigs.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Personally, I am more than excited to hear that DVD-ROM drives will   บ
 บ  be coming to home computers within the next year or two.  It could        บ
 บ  potentially kill the scene, but there are a million ways in which it      บ
 บ  could make things more convenient for life outside the scene.  For        บ
 บ  example, one will be able to put hours worth of quality music on just     บ
 บ  one DVD, and one will soon be able to purchase DVD movies (they'll be     บ
 บ  higher quality than current Laser-Discs, and cheaper too).  And if the    บ
 บ  cost of having these conveniences is the death of the scene, so be it.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Your thoughts are appreciated...                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      I've noticed recently that a bunch of groups bashing upon other       บ
 บ  groups by members of groups that are supposedly mature.  Now, I don't     บ
 บ  quite understand how those groups are mature if they don't have mature    บ
 บ  members.  I've also heard about people narqing each other in over one     บ
 บ  single release, over other such TRIVIAL matters as that.  I'd just like   บ
 บ  to emphasize that what we are doing in the scene is only for fun, as I'm  บ
 บ  sure thousands of people have already said before, and not to get         บ
 บ  people, not even your ENEMIES, into any trouble.  It's supposed to be     บ
 บ  friendly competition, what's wrong with that?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This also goes for people like Chris Carter, and I'm sure you're      บ
 บ  aware of his nice little reputation as a narq.  I also heard from a few   บ
 บ  people in Revolution X about Brawley being busted over some source code   บ
 บ  for some game or another, though I haven't seen any articles in any       บ
 บ  emags about it.  Why can't those people just calm down and wait a while   บ
 บ  so they can out do each other?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      They would certainly get back at their opposition just as well if     บ
 บ  they made them look foolish or slow, in a friendly way, rather than       บ
 บ  putting them behind bars, in a very UNfriendly way.  Hell, you might as   บ
 บ  well just go over to the person's house and shoot them!  Their families   บ
 บ  wouldn't be hurt any more or less by that!  In fact, you wouldn't         บ
 บ  absolutely destroy their reputation if you went over and killed them,     บ
 บ  rather than turning them in.  Again, the scene is for fun, it's not as    บ
 บ  if we're getting a salary for releasing warez in an illegal manner or     บ
 บ  anything.  Why do people get so pissed off about a stupid file?  Now, if  บ
 บ  they killed one of your relatives, I can see a reason for turning them    บ
 บ  in, but only a file?!  Come on, people, get it together and make the      บ
 บ  scene more fun, instead of a constant battle to the death against your    บ
 บ  competition.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are a lot of groups now a days.  I haven't been in the scene    บ
 บ  for that long, but I have heard stories about how it used to be.  I know  บ
 บ  that a long time ago, there weren't all these power trips going on        บ
 บ  within groups.  There was never any attempt at taking over a group (at    บ
 บ  least from what I've heard).                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I've been in the scene for a few years now, and what I see I don't    บ
 บ  really like.  I've been in a couple of groups.  I was in a local group,   บ
 บ  and I started as just a member (SysOp).  I moved up from being just a     บ
 บ  member to becoming the group's vice-president.  We were doing pretty      บ
 บ  good.  At first, we were kind of slow, but we moved up and had a few      บ
 บ  releases.  But then we were like any normal new group which didn't have   บ
 บ  many releases, and so we died.  It was a hard seven months, but we put    บ
 บ  every minute of our free time into the group.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The point I'm trying to make here is that, even though there are      บ
 บ  many groups in the scene which are supplying the warez, it doesn't mean   บ
 บ  they're all going to survive.  Even though they do die out, they still    บ
 บ  deserve some credit.  We put in hours and hours a day trying to make a    บ
 บ  small group a good one.  But we don't give credit where it is due.  We    บ
 บ  always end up bypassing a small group and going towards the bigger ones   บ
 บ  due to reputation.  It doesn't matter how long a group has been in the    บ
 บ  scene, or by how many releases they've had, but what does matter is how   บ
 บ  good their releases are.  The saying "Quality over Quantity" is taken     บ
 บ  for granted.  Many groups in the scene say that they release all quality  บ
 บ  warez.  How about the releases that are all a bunch of shit?  It's not    บ
 บ  how good a group does in releasing, it's how good their releases are,     บ
 บ  and on how much they try to make the scene better.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Join Channel #Oasis96 Today!                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Glycerine,                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      I agree with you completely on the note of quality warez.  However,   บ
 บ  I disagree with your assumption of "how it used to be".  It's a general   บ
 บ  misconception that the scene of long past is somehow better than the one  บ
 บ  today.  Even back in the Commodore 64 days, there were groups, and they   บ
 บ  bickered and fought amongst themselves.  To ignore that fact and to say   บ
 บ  that it never happened is ludicrous.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I also have some other advice for you, this might sound kind of       บ
 บ  stupid, but to tell you the truth, one of these days, you'll probably     บ
 บ  merge your small group into a big group just for the "reputation".  It    บ
 บ  sounds hypocritical, but I've seen it a dozen times already just in the   บ
 บ  past year.  Take care, and remember, if it's not fun.. don't do it.       บ

                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Groups today seem to be getting an ever crappier and crappier         บ
 บ  attitude.  They get a few couriers and maybe a tiny bit of name           บ
 บ  recognition and suddenly they think they're really hot stuff and get      บ
 บ  major elitist attitudes.  I have a simple question for those faggots,     บ
 บ  who the heck do they think they're impressing?  In order to help out a    บ
 บ  few of these pathetic wannabes, I'm writing this neat little letter with  บ
 บ  a couple suggestions.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, you might thinking - who the heck is this guy?!  Good      บ
 บ  question!  You've probably seen one of my bots at one time or another     บ
 บ  (XanthDCC), which I've been told are usually the top bots online          บ
 บ  whenever I put one up, mainly because they're packed with about 250 megs  บ
 บ  each and operate over a T3 and I actually know what I'm doing, unlike     บ
 บ  most people who type /plist.  Oh, there was this little thing I did for   บ
 บ  a while as head courier/coordinator for Impulse a while back, which was   บ
 บ  MindCrash, but then it merged into Digital Traders while I was gone and   บ
 บ  I quit, but that's a really long and boring story.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Let's start with a few of my suggestions on channel modes.  My        บ
 บ  general feeling is that +i channels suck.  When I was doing anything      บ
 บ  with Impulse, I always tried to keep it -i, because without doing that,   บ
 บ  you don't see a lot of new faces.  AND, when it's +i, a day with          บ
 บ  netsplits or a broken bot can be terrible for your members.  A recent     บ
 บ  example of such would be how none of PTA (Power Trading Arsenal)          บ
 บ  couriers seem to be able to get into the channel because their bots       บ
 บ  suck.  Anyone with half a brain can tell that they DON'T want this to     บ
 บ  happen to them under *ANY* circumstances.  Keep your channel -i if        บ
 บ  you're a new group and rapidly expanding.  If you're an established       บ
 บ  group, keeping the channel that follows your group name (i.e. If your     บ
 บ  group is LEET COURIERS, the channel would be #LEET) -i is a good idea.    บ
 บ  Keeping a public relations person in the channel at all times is a        บ
 บ  definite plus.  Of course, a +i channel that only members know of and     บ
 บ  have access to would also be a great idea.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With all the new groups popping up, undoubtedly, almost all of them   บ
 บ  lack some organization skills.  Weeeeeeeeee!  Use a spreadsheet or        บ
 บ  something like it to help organize things.  I learned this little tip     บ
 บ  from Headbanger, and it was a good idea, except for the fact that I       บ
 บ  didn't use Windows.  Having the sheet on the same computer you courier    บ
 บ  from is a good idea.  Multitasking is a MUST for any courier.  Organize   บ
 บ  this in whichever manner *YOU* feel most comfortable with, and you'll be  บ
 บ  able to remove bad or or idle members with relative ease.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Having the *SECURE* email addresses of ALL members is also            บ
 บ  necessary.  Put them in your address book if the need arises.  If         บ
 บ  there's a handle and realname slot, put their position in the real name   บ
 บ  slot and handle in the handle slot.  This makes things a HECK of a lot    บ
 บ  easier for you.  Send out frequent mailers just to give some support,     บ
 บ  rules updates (read on for more on rules), or other important info (new   บ
 บ  FTP sites, couriers, bots, etc.)                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is something that a lot of people don't do, but I would like to  บ
 บ  see done a lot more, it's just something that bugs me to death.  Get a    บ
 บ  copy of phoenix and add your group name to the top.  It helps give your   บ
 บ  group a much more "polished" look.            Onto the subject of IRC     บ
 บ  Couriers, IRC is a great method to spread a lot of files to a lot of      บ
 บ  people really fast, albeit you usually can't move a whole lot.  First     บ
 บ  off, people always seem to be addicted to this great auto-plist feature.  บ
 บ  I personally think it's irritating as heck, and altogether useless.  If   บ
 บ  you have something good, load up TWO bots, one with it on and one with    บ
 บ  it off.  When you PLIST, your queue will jam up immediately, etc.  A few  บ
 บ  other notes, set your Auto-Ptime way high, to about 20 minutes or so.     บ
 บ  If you're offering a bunch of 10 meg files, plist'ing just to tell        บ
 บ  people all your slots are full and the queue is jammed up every 5         บ
 บ  minutes is stupid.  Also, make SURE you have a MINSPEED!  But, make sure  บ
 บ  that your provider can push your minspeed, if it's 3 and you can't get    บ
 บ  more than a 2.5 because there's no bandwidth, it does no one any good.    บ
 บ  Finally, set your queue down to about 5 if you're offering large files.   บ
 บ  A 2 hour wait in a queue of 10 or 20 just results in false queue's (a     บ
 บ  ghosted queue - offline people in your queue) and a lot of frustration.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you leave your bot up for a long time, XDCC SAVE and restart       บ
 บ  frequently, when IRC splits occur, phoenix screwes up and you'll get      บ
 บ  queues of like 11/5.  Yuck.  Make sure you detach your session!  (If you  บ
 บ  don't know how to do this - DON'T IRC OFFER).  IRC is extremely           บ
 บ  inefficient.  When the PCPU and JCPU times get up to like 8:12, and       บ
 บ  everyone else is at 57, your ISP administrator knows something is up.     บ
 บ  If you have no idea what I'm talking about, hit "w".  That shows the CPU  บ
 บ  percentage that you are taking up.  PCPU is present usage, and JCPU is    บ
 บ  peak usage.  IRC typically doesn't relinquish anything on the PCPU when   บ
 บ  you get it up there.  6 slots on a crappy machine with a T1 is enough to  บ
 บ  get this through the stratosphere.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      FTP couriering is not nearly as conspicuous as IRC, because your CPU  บ
 บ  usage is much lower.  But, diskspace fluctuations are much greater, so    บ
 บ  hope that your provider has a fast SCSI disk. =)  I've erased and         บ
 บ  written in excess of a gig a day when I was still into couriering a lot,  บ
 บ  without blinking an eye.  First off, *ALWAYS* use NcFTP v2.3.0 (I think   บ
 บ  that's the most recent).  This version stores your logins and passwords,  บ
 บ  and has lots of nifty features.  If you *MUST* use FTP, NEVER EVER EVER   บ
 บ  do a "ftp my.site.name.here.com", you just showed everyone on your        บ
 บ  provider what the name of the FTP site you're going to is!  Duh!  With    บ
 บ  FTP, just make sure to dupe check well, and upload an NFO file.  That     บ
 บ  should be about it.  FTP is really quite simple from a technical          บ
 บ  standpoint, from the couriering standpoint, it's tough with fast FTP      บ
 บ  sites.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This one is my favorite topic, and I'm hoping this inspires a few     บ
 บ  groups to do something!  Anonymous FTP.  While it's typically             บ
 บ  disregarded as being lame and crappy by a lot of groups, in reality that  บ
 บ  is totally wrong.  Since most couriers use hacked accounts, FTP site      บ
 บ  busts aren't really an immediated danger to you.  You don't compete on    บ
 บ  an anonymous FTP site!  It's easy, when you get a file, unzip it, grap a  บ
 บ  DIZ and NFO, login to the FTP site, and upload!  No competition, no       บ
 บ  "need for speed", just pure plain couriering fun.         Here's how you  บ
 บ  can create an anonymous FTP site.  First off, you must find a writable    บ
 บ  directory.  Something not found in the /incoming is preferable.  Now,     บ
 บ  make a directory.  Like, "mkdir tmp" or something.  Now, erase it         บ
 บ  ("rmdir tmp").  This is a test for mkdir and rmdir permissions.  Making   บ
 บ  a directory with a SPACE in it is always an EXCELLENT idea, to check      บ
 บ  filename acceptance.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you can remove the dir, continue on.  If you can't, find another   บ
 บ  FTP site.  That one is NO GOOD.  Now, remake the dir and upload a file.   บ
 บ  Check the speed you got, make sure it's high.  Erase the file, if you     บ
 บ  can't - forget about this FTP site.  If you can, download the file to be  บ
 บ  sure the FTP site allows downloads.  If all is good, upload 200 megs      บ
 บ  worth of GARBAGE, make sure *ALL* of it uploads, then erase it.  This     บ
 บ  sounds stupid, but it's a disk space check, and is essential.  If it      บ
 บ  fills the disk, forget that FTP site.  If it doesn't, you just found an   บ
 บ  anonymous FTP site!                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Making directories is the fun part!  NEVER use the words "warez",     บ
 บ  "appz", "userz", "gamez", "sitez", or "talkz".  These are DEAD GIVEAWAYS  บ
 บ  to FTPSearch or Archie users.  Something like "gaming", and               บ
 บ  "applications" are best. "G_mez", "A_pz", etc. also work quite nicely.    บ
 บ  High ASCII root directories are great for security, but work poorly for   บ
 บ  many reasons.  A blank space directory is much preferable, or a           บ
 บ  "<TAB><space>" is nice.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Your FTP site is now ready!  Upload only good files, as this isn't a  บ
 บ  competitive thing.  Keep the disk usage to about 400 megs or less, and    บ
 บ  erase files frequently.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So you followed all my guidlines and still no one cares about your    บ
 บ  group?  Just keep at it, people will start to listen up soon.  Recruit    บ
 บ  new couriers and FTP site operators, people will trickle in.  Put         บ
 บ  applications in *ONE* slot at the end of a DCC offer list that's PACKED   บ
 บ  with fast good warez, and put them on your anonymous FTP site.  Make      บ
 บ  sure to have an auto-responder to your public channel.  Keep              บ
 บ  knowledgeable and helpful people on hand at all times to talk to people   บ
 บ  who are interested.  You could even recruit a few good couriers from      บ
 บ  other groups to help out.  If you can get someone in a more established   บ
 บ  group to put a few files on your FTP site, that will always help.  Hang   บ
 บ  out in as many release group channels as you can, and have members apply  บ
 บ  to release groups.  Having your members inside a release group equates    บ
 บ  to more tags for you and faster files.  But, above all, have fun.  Warez  บ
 บ  are not all your life, they're a hobby.  Have fun and best of luck!       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Xanthos                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Xanthos,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thanks for telling us all about how to start a courier group and how  บ
 บ  we can all make good anonymous FTP sites.  I'm sure that it is all very   บ
 บ  informative, and if I ever feel like starting a courier group, I'll be    บ
 บ  sure to send you a Christmas card :)                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ

 บ  files over the net or BBSs, some of us haven't gotten the time to ask     บ
 บ  people what is happening in the scene.  RCN informs us with a             บ
 บ  professional approach and cool texts, hot interviews, unlike ones that    บ
 บ  we've had to read in other e-mags.  Since RCN returned from its 3-month   บ
 บ  holiday, I can say that it is getting better by the week, collecting new  บ
 บ  writers.  From the first amateur number we now have a pro e-zine which    บ
 บ  rules over them all.  Also, I would like to congradulte the editors for   บ
 บ  putting texts with lots of humor in it, despite the fact that they have   บ
 บ  nothing to do with warez.  It shouldn't be just strictly a warez mag      บ
 บ  because that would be boring.  Reading a few last articles (Especially    บ
 บ  TKRP's love adventure, I laughed my ass off!) that are funny is good!     บ
 บ  Keep up the good work!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ

 บ  Dear Brab,                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Along with 50 other reasons for returning, a significant one was      บ
 บ  that we felt that the warez public was not being properly informed about  บ
 บ  the events that encircled it.  Other e-mags just weren't giving the       บ
 บ  scene all that it deserved.  However, like you said, having a little fun  บ
 บ  never hurts.  Once we feel that we have accomplished our task of          บ
 บ  informing the public about the events of the week in a more than          บ
 บ  adequate manner, we see nothing wrong with adding a little dash of humor  บ
 บ  here, and another there.  It's what sets us apart.  Nevertheless, not     บ
 บ  all people perceive our "Mad RCN" articles as humor.  I will take this    บ
 บ  opportunity to apologize to all those that were "exploited" and didn't    บ
 บ  think it was funny.  You people need a life.  And to the people that      บ
 บ  were published and thought it was amusing, that's what we think too.  So  บ
 บ  finally, remember, it's all for fun and is in good humor.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since you guys were doing some interviews about people getting        บ
 บ  busted, I was wondering if you would know anything about minors.  I'm     บ
 บ  16.  If someone narqed on my BBS, would the penalties be much less        บ
 บ  harsh?                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Overkill                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Overkill,                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You don't want to get busted, small penalties or not.  It's just not  บ
 บ  a fun thing.  If you're over 18, generally you'll be fined off your ass   บ
 บ  and have all your equipment seized for good.  You might also have to      บ
 บ  spend some time in jail, not to mention your record will not be wiped.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Being that you're 16, I would say that you wouldn't be spending any   บ
 บ  time in jail, and if they did seize your equipment, it would probably     บ
 บ  only be temporary.   However, a common act that the FBI (or whoever it    บ
 บ  is that got you) will do is go to your school.  That's not fun.  I knew   บ
 บ  this one guy that got busted and the FBI ended up going to his school     บ
 บ  with him and made him give a speech to every class in the school stating  บ
 บ  what he did, why it was wrong, and why copyright infringement isn't       บ
 บ  cool.  Of course, if you don't want to do that, you could always just     บ
 บ  pay them a few thousand dollars.  Take your pick.  Not to mention, your   บ
 บ  parents will probably have your head on a stick within a matter of        บ
 บ  minutes.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Ultimately, you don't want to get busted.  But you're in the scene    บ
 บ  and not only that, you have a BBS.  You need to take responsibility for   บ
 บ  yourself and know that there is always a chance that you will get         บ
 บ  busted.  By keeping your BBS up, you are accepting that fact and          บ
 บ  accepting the fact that you could get busted at any time.  You should     บ
 บ  know that laws are different depending on the state in which you are in.  บ
 บ  To find out more, you could call your city hall and find out about their  บ
 บ  policies.  You could also GOPHER into the LIBRARY OF CONGRESS on the      บ
 บ  Internet for more information.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  #warez and #warez2.  I quickly learned that most of the guys around were  บ
 บ  cool and this 'new found' warez tool was invaluable to everyone.  When a  บ
 บ  ware was released, it was quickly put up for XDCC and was quickly spread  บ
 บ  by everyone.  Now, with the growth that the Internet has seen in the      บ
 บ  past year, it is easy to see why he is experiencing these problems; a     บ
 บ  million people on IRC.  When he asks 'WHAT THE FUCK ARE THEY FOR?'        บ
 บ  Well, I can answer this : To allow little 15-year old fuck heads to       บ
 บ  think they're big shit.  That's it.  With the exception of the first      บ
 บ  #warez channels, this is what it's always been for.  This was way before  บ
 บ  my time.  Now, not even #warez has warez.  We talk about OJ's genital     บ

 บ  comment is to be directed to a specific group, I don't feel it necessary  บ
 บ  to exploit it in front of the entire scene in the E-Mag.  Instead, I      บ
 บ  think it would be more appropriate for that person to e-mail the group    บ
 บ  leaders directly.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Daviolator           บ
 บ    Subject  : Napalm DEAD???            Affiliation : Napalm Leader        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The general consensus of the scene toward Napalm is that it is no   บ
 บ        longer doing as well as it did in the past.  One can even go so     บ
 บ        far as to say that Napalm is dead because it is no longer           บ
 บ        releasing on a regular basis.  Do you believe that Napalm is dead,  บ
 บ        or is dying?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : No, that is absolutely not true.  As you can see, besides           บ
 บ        Prestige, every other games group in the scene is also suffering    บ
 บ        from a release slump.  Prestige is the games releasing force at     บ
 บ        the moment, but I think Napalm will be able to take some quality    บ
 บ        releases from Prestige here and there.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Less than 2 weeks ago, both Napalm and Prestige released Battle     บ
 บ        Arena : Toshinden, but both groups happened to release an           บ
 บ        identical crack.  Not only has Prestige accused Napalm of stealing  บ
 บ        the crack for Battle Arena : Toshinden, Prestige has backed it      บ
 บ        with evidence (RCN #16).  I want to see *YOU*, the leader of        บ
 บ        Napalm, explain why the cracks for Battle Arena : Toshinden from    บ
 บ        both groups are exactly the identical, even down to the time        บ
 บ        stamps.  Did Napalm steal the Prestige crack, or did it not?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Well, I really can't answer question.  It's not that I don't want   บ
 บ        to answer the question, but I really don't know the whole story.    บ
 บ        I have been taking it easy as of late and I only know as much as    บ
 บ        the average person.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There are a few indicators and pointers here and there that inform  บ
 บ        the leader that their group is not doing too well.  For release     บ
 บ        groups, one can say that a group is doing horribly if it doesn't    บ
 บ        release in a long period of time.  Napalm hasn't released in        บ
 บ        almost 3 weeks, and I consider that a long period of time.  Also,   บ
 บ        when members of a group flood out to join other groups, I too       บ
 บ        consider that to be a bad sign.  Many of Napalm's crackers have     บ
 บ        left Napalm to join Prestige, one such cracker is Lost Soul.  How   บ
 บ        has his absence and the absence of other former Napalm members      บ
 บ        effected the group as a whole?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Loyalty.  If there is no loyalty in a group, then the group can     บ
 บ        never do well.  When Napalm was doing well, everyone was asking to  บ
 บ        join, but once Prestige started releasing, everyone wanted to be a  บ
 บ        Prestige member.  I feel that flooding back and forth between       บ
 บ        groups is extremely lame.  Napalm still has many loyal members,     บ
 บ        and I thank those who are loyal for sticking with the group         บ
 บ        through the tough times.  Napalm may no longer be the #1 games      บ
 บ        group, but we surely do like to think of ourselves as the #2 games  บ
 บ        group.  As for the fact that Napalm has not released yet, people    บ
 บ        need not worry, the releases will be coming shortly.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : In last week's interview with Shatter Star, I asked him why Napalm  บ
 บ        was not releasing, and he said that it was not releasing because    บ
 บ        Napalm was apparently testing the "LOYALTY" of the members.  When   บ
 บ        he said that, I assumed that Shatter Star was taking the role of a  บ
 บ        loyal Napalm member, but not even a week has passed, and he's       บ
 บ        already ditched Napalm for Prestige.  It seems to me that he no     บ
 บ        longer believes that Napalm is refusing to release because it       บ
 บ        wishes to test its members.  What are your feelings on his          บ
 บ        resignation, and what are your feelings toward him?  Has his        บ
 บ        resignation effected the standing of the group?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Like I said, people tend to hop from one group to another because   บ
 บ        they want to be in group that is releasing a lot.  What can I say?  บ
 บ        Napalm is not doing well at the moment, so all the unloyal members  บ
 บ        jump ship.  You can't put a choke on them, it's their decision to   บ
 บ        do whatever they want.  Personally, this is just more about having  บ
 บ        fun then anything else.  Why should I get stressed out over these   บ
 บ        things?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There is a parallel between the old Napalm Consoles and the         บ
 บ        current Napalm PC, both groups were at one point in time, a very    บ
 บ        strong releasing force, but both started to release less as time    บ
 บ        passed.  When Napalm Consoles could no longer release, you merged   บ
 บ        Napalm Consoles into another consoles group called Sneakers, and    บ
 บ        then you headed off to try your luck at running a successful games  บ
 บ        group on another platform, the PC, and thus Napalm PC was created.  บ
 บ        Now that Napalm PC is close to dying, will you merge it into        บ
 บ        Prestige, and then perhaps move on to releasing games on another    บ
 บ        platform?  You should try your luck starting Napalm MAC, there's a  บ
 บ        lot less competition in releasing Macintosh games...                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Hehe, that is kind of funny to hear.  Napalm Consoles wasn't even   บ
 บ        close to dying when I merged it into Sneakers.  The reason why I    บ
 บ        merged Napalm Consoles into Sneakers was because the other Napalm   บ
 บ        leaders and I were too busy to run things, so I decided to merge    บ
 บ        Napalm into a consoles group that was no longer releasing as well   บ
 บ        as it used to, but still had a good reputation.  I really hope      บ
 บ        that Napalm PC will not need to merge into another games group.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Well, you were looking for a consoles group that was slowing down,  บ
 บ        but had a good reputation?  Razor 1911 is a perfect counterpart to  บ
 บ        Sneakers.  Razor 1911 is a games group that is slowing down, but    บ
 บ        they have a great reputation, is Napalm considering a merge with    บ
 บ        Razor 1911, or is a merge out of question?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Napalm Consoles didn't have a problem with merging into Sneakers    บ
 บ        because most members of both groups were good friends.  I highly    บ
 บ        doubt that Napalm PC will merge into Razor 1911, there isn't much   บ
 บ        love between the two groups.  But then again, you never know, who   บ
 บ        would have ever thought Nexus would merge into Razor 1911, or that  บ
 บ        Dynamix would merge into Prestige?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does Napalm get most of their releases?  I've heard rumors      บ
 บ        that Napalm is a group that specializes in getting releases         บ
 บ        through store pick ups.  Suppliers who do store pick ups can be     บ
 บ        very effective, but most groups that only have suppliers that do    บ
 บ        store pick ups usually suffer from a bad reputation, an example of  บ
 บ        such would be ROR (Release on Rampage).  Is that also the case      บ
 บ        with Napalm?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : I would say that store pick ups is one of Napalm's most effective   บ
 บ        ways in getting releases.  However, now that my buddy Shadow        บ
 บ        Master is doing store pick ups for Prestige, it's made Napalm's     บ
 บ        job a lot tougher.  Shadow Master, you're the best man!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Was Shadow Master ever a member of Napalm, or any groups you've     บ
 บ        been affiliated with?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : I was with Shadow Master in Phoenix.  He was also in Napalm         บ
 บ        Consoles ever since it started, but then he left to start up SWAT   บ
 บ        Consoles (Special Warez Acquisition Team) with his friend Cyber     บ
 บ        Christ.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Wow, I remember Cyber Christ, Digital Messiah (my friend who        บ
 บ        taught me about the scene) told me that Cyber Christ was "Cool and  บ
 บ        Elite", back before I even had a chance to start memorizing group   บ
 บ        acronyms.  Anyway, when you started Napalm PC, was Shadow Master    บ
 บ        in any PC games groups?  If not, why did you not ask him to come    บ
 บ        work with you in Napalm?  And if you did ask, I assume that he      บ
 บ        must have rejected your offer, and if so, why?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Shadow Master was not in any PC groups at the time Napalm PC        บ
 บ        started because he was too busy with SWAT Consoles.  I did ask      บ
 บ        Shadow Master to join Napalm PC, but he said that he had no         บ
 บ        interest in the lame CD-Ripping scene.  He said the PC scene is     บ
 บ        not the same as the good old floppy days.  Next thing I know, he    บ
 บ        joins Razor 1911.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : May be Shadow Master changed his mind?  Anyway, I joined #Napalm a  บ
 บ        few minutes ago, and on the channel topic, it said :                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ        *** Topic for #napalm: THIS WEEK WILL BE NAPALM'S COME BACK WEEK!   บ
 บ        *** Topic for #napalm set by Prophet_ on Jun  4 16:28:39            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : What is Napalm planning to do differently this week that will make  บ
 บ        it "come back"?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : We plan to release one game more than we have for the last 3        บ
 บ        weeks.  I would say that releasing is a positive thing, wouldn't    บ
 บ        you agree?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  NPM : Releasing will do Napalm a ton of good, and that is positive for    บ
 บ        the group, assuming the release is not a dupe and is fully          บ
 บ        functional.  However, the core of Napalm's cracking force has left  บ
 บ        Napalm to join Prestige.  If/when Napalm does get a release, how    บ
 บ        will it get cracked?  Napalm wouldn't happen to be planning to      บ
 บ        release a game that is not cracked properly, would it?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Well, we still have some kick ass crackers in Napalm such as        บ
 บ        Wolverine, and others whom we cannot name because they do not wish  บ
 บ        to be revealed.  If you have noticed our past couple of releases,   บ
 บ        there weren't any fuck ups.  We were so confident that we started   บ
 บ        fixing other groups releases such as Hybrid's release of Lemmings   บ
 บ        Paintball for Windows 95.                                           บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Frost                บ
 บ    Subject  : Digital Traders DEAD!!!   Affiliation : Digital Council      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Digital is an awesome courier group in the recent months, but I've  บ
 บ        been informed by some personal friends of the network that Digital  บ
 บ        have retired, is that rumor true?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DGT : Yes, it is true.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : It was doing extremely well as a courier group, and was gaining     บ
 บ        respectability within the scene by leaps and bounds?  Why did       บ
 บ        Digital retire?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DGT : The presidents of Digital, Devast and Silent Mobius decided to      บ
 บ        retire from the group.  As to the reason why, I myself am not       บ
 บ        sure, we have yet to inform the group.                              บ

 บ        Digital?  Are you telling me he does not have faith in himself to   บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DGT : Blitzkrieg is a great leader, the only problem with Blitzkrieg is   บ
 บ        that he is not online too often.  If there is a new group formed    บ

 บ        it.                                                                 บ

 บ        group?  Perhaps Digital might merge into RiSC (Rise in Superior     บ

 บ        I am 100% sure that each of our traders is competent enough to      บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        still be up this summer.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What does Amnesia have to say about the death of Digital?  After    บ
 บ        all, the courier contest between Amnesia vs. Digital might have     บ
 บ        harbored some harsh feelings which could lead to conflicts down     บ
 บ        the road.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DGT : I wouldn't say that Amnesia is the arch-enemy of Digital, most of   บ
 บ        the members of Amnesia and Digital are good friends.  Digital       บ
 บ        merely competed with Amnesia.  As for what Amnesia says about the   บ
 บ        death of Digital, that's not for me to say.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I consider you a coordinator in Digital, after all, you were the    บ
 บ        one that helped update the nfos.  Where will you be going now that  บ
 บ        Digital is dead, which courier group are you seeking after?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DGT : I'm pretty open to things right now, I think that Silent Mobius     บ
 บ        and Devast may have some plans for the group, we are not the type   บ
 บ        that would leave our members lying around, we will probably start   บ
 บ        a small group for our traders and move on from there.  Right now,   บ
 บ        I am not thinking about where I might go, but I am thinking about   บ
 บ        how I should get my traders into a new courier group.               บ
