 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Tok                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Defacto/Sodom             Affiliation : Sodom Leader         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Sodom has been showing its releasing potential in the recent weeks  บ
 บ        by releasing tons of software, and some may even consider that      บ
 บ        Sodom is now one of the top 5 utils groups.  Do you feel that this  บ
 บ        is true?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Yes, of course it's true.  We have been working hard 10 to 14       บ
 บ        hours a day since we formed the group on July 11, 1995.  We know    บ
 บ        the scene well now and many people know us.  We have worked hard    บ
 บ        and long for our reputation, and that is part of the reason for     บ
 บ        our success.  Of course, we've had conflicts with other groups,     บ
 บ        but they've left already, and we've been preserved.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I know that Sodom is a Russian group, and that DOD (Drink or Die)   บ
 บ        is also a Russian group that advertises itself as the "Russian      บ
 บ        Warez Bears".  Do you believe that Sodom is the true Russian Warez  บ
 บ        Bears, and it has conquered that section of Europe indefinitely?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Hmm... this is a really long story, Sodom and DOD that is.  What    บ
 บ        can I say, we have somewhat of a competition in Russia that         บ
 บ        stemmed when Sodom and DOD were formed, and, now we're winning, so  บ
 บ        DOD is really going down hill.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What competition was there between Sodom and DOD when Sodom first   บ
 บ        started, and what do you mean when you say that DOD is really       บ
 บ        going down hill?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Actually, when we were first formed, there was no competition,      บ
 บ        because it was in 1995, and back then, DOD was really famous.  It   บ
 บ        think it was the best in the scene when it came to utils.  So, we   บ
 บ        can't really talk about competition in 1995, but then, after all    บ
 บ        organization questions and communication conflicts were worked      บ
 บ        out, we moved to IRC, and began to work work work.  As I said, we   บ
 บ        worked from 10-14 hours a day.  Internet in Russia is really bad,   บ
 บ        the connection speeds are extremely slow, especially with people    บ
 บ        that are still on 9600s, so uploading is difficult.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did Jimmy Jamez leave the scene?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Why?  Well, Jimmy Jamez, the leader of DOD, left the scene about    บ
 บ        80% of the way.  He got work in Moscow, and he didn't care about    บ
 บ        DOD any more, maybe some old seniors, but not Jimmy Jamez, and      บ
 บ        some suppliers, joined other release groups, and so half the        บ
 บ        people in the current DOD.NFO are actually NOT IN DOD.  As you can  บ
 บ        see, DOD's releases of the past two months haven't been working     บ
 บ        ones.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many people know you as the leader of Sodom, but many also know     บ
 บ        that you were an editor of Defacto, and I use the word "were" in    บ
 บ        the past tense, why did you leave Defacto?  Earlier, you informed   บ
 บ        me that it was because of the Sodom Project.  What is the Sodom     บ
 บ        Project?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : This really sucks, but Sodom was forced to drop the Sodom Project.  บ
 บ        3 or 4 council members from Defacto didn't want to be in the Sodom  บ
 บ        Project, and it became like the U.S. Revolution.  I was the main    บ
 บ        organizer of Defacto, and after this decision, I downgraded myself  บ
 บ        to writer, but RCN came back, and I think we gave you a chance to   บ
 บ        monopolize all the warez e-mags in the scene, and I think you did,  บ
 บ        and that's why Defacto #8 will be the future of e-mags!  I think I  บ
 บ        will upgrade my position back one day, but not yet, this is a hard  บ
 บ        time for me, I have exams in the university, and Sodom is taking    บ
 บ        up much of my time.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you will one day become the Sodom editor again?  What exactly    บ
 บ        was the Sodom Project?  And why do you feel that Defacto #8 will    บ
 บ        be the future of e-mags?  What about Defacto #8 will make it so     บ
 บ        revolutionary?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Heh, okay, well, if you don't already know, Defacto was originally  บ
 บ        started by Sodom, so the founders were NetRunner, IPggi, and me.    บ
 บ        All the people who write or do anything for Defacto are in Sodom,   บ
 บ        so that's why it was called the Sodom Project.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When will you be returning to Defacto?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Yes, very soon, after my exams are over, I think I will be able to  บ
 บ        return to Defacto as a *SECRET*, but anyway, #8 will be             บ
 บ        revolutionary. And do you want to know why?  Well, because it will  บ
 บ        have good coding, SVGA graphics, and many features.  Anyway, I      บ
 บ        like this competition between RCN and Defacto, but nearly everyone  บ
 บ        thinks that RCN is ruling the e-mag scene, and we are some small    บ
 บ        shit, but remember, we are only on issue #8!                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I'm glad to see that Defacto is doing something to improve its      บ
 บ        image.  However, the idea of an SVGA e-mag is by no means a new     บ
 บ        one, the Demo and Art scene has been implementing it for years      บ
 บ        now.  What makes you think that the public will perceive it as      บ
 บ        such a revolutionary change?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Hmm.. well, first I'm not the coder, our coder is Captain Power,    บ
 บ        he built this in C++, Assembly, and a little Pascal source.         บ
 บ        Second, our e-mag will be much better with compression, not 2.X MB  บ
 บ        like RCN.  We also have a good VGA artist.  Many new writers        บ
 บ        applied for Defacto last week.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : RCN's size is a direct result of the many articles it presents to   บ
 บ        the scene every week.  Coding and art is but an iota of the entire  บ
 บ        EXE size.  Will this not be the opposite in Defacto?  Defacto has   บ
 บ        just a fraction of the articles that RCN does, and, assuming all    บ
 บ        goes well, Defacto will be spending much more space on mere coding  บ
 บ        and SVGA art, right?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOK : Hehehe, naw man, Defacto is COMPRESSED!!!  EVERYTHING IS!!!         บ

 บ    Reporter : Xenon                     Interviewee : Flexor               บ
 บ    Subject  : Legacy Revival            Affiliation : Legacy President     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many of us know that the games group known as Legacy died a few     บ
 บ        months ago when its leaders left the scene to pursue other          บ
 บ        interests.  However, there are some rumors that Legacy is coming    บ
 บ        back up, is that true?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : Yes, that's true, Legacy is coming back up.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So are you telling me that the former leaders of Legacy have come   บ
 บ        back from the retirement to restart Legacy?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : No, the former leaders of Legacy have left the warez scene and I    บ
 บ        am merely restarting the group with new members.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Who were the former leaders of Legacy?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : The original founders of Legacy was Rebel Chicken and Hitex.  I'm   บ
 บ        not sure if they have left the scene completely, but I know that    บ
 บ        they are currently editors of a warez e-mag called Reality Check    บ
 บ        Network.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you have permission from Rebel Chicken and Hitex to start a      บ
 บ        group using the Legacy name?  Wouldn't they be upset with the fact  บ
 บ        that someone else is taking advantage of the Legacy name in order   บ
 บ        to promote a new group that had nothing to do with the old?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : Yes, I asked Rebel Chicken and Hitex about using the Legacy name,   บ
 บ        and they did not seem upset with it at all.  They only showed       บ
 บ        apathy and indifference toward the fact that I was starting a       บ
 บ        group called Legacy.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are any of the former Legacy suppliers a part of this new Legacy?   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : No, but they are welcome to join if they wish to do so.  I need     บ
 บ        all the suppliers I can get my hands on.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are any of the former Legacy members a part of this new Legacy?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : No, and I think that's just too bad.  I think that none of the old  บ
 บ        Legacy members have joined the new Legacy because they have yet to  บ
 บ        hear that the group is coming back up.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : As is common knowledge, Legacy died off under the leadership of     บ
 บ        Rebel Chicken and Hitex because they left the scene, what will you  บ
 บ        do differently this time that will make Legacy survive and do       บ
 บ        better than it did before?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : I will try to make sure that the members of the group stays         บ
 บ        informed with all the group happenings.  I will try to be a good    บ
 บ        leader.  I have no thoughts.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Will Legacy be releasing only games, or only utils, or both games   บ
 บ        and utils?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : I have discussed that with the group and we've come to the          บ
 บ        conclusion that we will stick to releasing only games because it's  บ
 บ        too much of a hassle to release both games and utils.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Some might consider it EASIER to release both games and utils       บ
 บ        because crappy utils are easier to find and release.  Wouldn't it   บ
 บ        be easier for you if you made Legacy a utils only group, or a       บ
 บ        group that released both games and utils?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : The utils scene is currently monopolized by groups such as PWA      บ
 บ        (Pirates with Attitudes) and DOD (Drink or Die).  The best games    บ
 บ        release group at the moment is Prestige.  I don't know why I want   บ
 บ        to make Legacy a games only group, but I just have a feeling that   บ
 บ        starting a games group would be good for now.  I have already       บ
 บ        tried doing utils before, but to no avail.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned earlier that NONE of the original Legacy members      บ
 บ        have joined the new Legacy.  I can then infer that none of the      บ
 บ        former Legacy crackers and coders are not with you either, will     บ
 บ        your new Legacy have the same quality of coding found in the late   บ
 บ        Legacy?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : Well, if the old crackers and coders come back to Legacy, then we   บ
 บ        will have the same quality as before.  They were really good at     บ
 บ        it, and it would be very hard to go back to their level.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : In Mortality's latest release, Omnipage Pro v7.0 for Windows 95, I  บ
 บ        found that according to the nfo file included in the release, the   บ
 บ        supplier of release was named Legacy.  Also included in the         บ
 บ        release is a legacy.nfo, do you have any information concerning     บ
 บ        this matter?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : No, actually I didn't know about this until you informed me now.    บ
 บ        Thanks for telling me.. :).                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where are most of the members of this new Legacy located at?  Will  บ
 บ        this new Legacy be a US group, or a European group?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LGC : I Live in Sweden, but we have many members that live in the US, so  บ
 บ        you can say that our group is very spread out.                      บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Met                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Rebels                    Affiliation : Rebels Council       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where do you see Rebels today, compared to other utils groups in    บ
 บ        the scene such as DOD (Drink or Die) and PWA (Pirates with          บ
 บ        Attitudes)?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Well, PWA has almost always been the biggest utils group in the     บ
 บ        scene, and still are.  DOD has been going down hill lately, but     บ
 บ        DOD is still made up of many good members.  Rebels is a very        บ
 บ        strong group, but we are not yet as big as PWA.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why do you feel that Rebels is not as good as PWA?  What makes PWA  บ
 บ        better than Rebels?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Well, I feel that Rebels is comparable to PWA at this moment,       บ
 บ        however, PWA has been very big for several years now and Rebels     บ
 บ        has not been as big for as long a time.  In my opinion, that makes  บ
 บ        PWA the better group since I believe that experience is very        บ
 บ        important.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How will Rebels go about gaining such experience, do you merely     บ
 บ        get this experience by being the older group?  As far as I know,    บ
 บ        isn't Rebels OLDER than PWA?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Yes, Rebels is a very old group and is even older that Razor 1911.  บ
 บ        Rebels has been around ever since 1984 when it was a group          บ
 บ        specialized in the Amiga scene.  Right after I first bought my PC,  บ
 บ        Omnibuz and I decided to start Rebels PC as a demo group.  We've    บ
 บ        been releasing PC utils for almost 2 years now, but the first year  บ
 บ        of releasing was really bad.  Many of the members in Rebels are     บ
 บ        former members of groups such as Nexus, Razor 1911, and TRSi.  We   บ
 บ        feel ready to rock DOD and PWA.  The scene should really watch out  บ
 บ        for us now that Pantera has merged into Rebels.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did Rebels switch from coding demos to releasing PC utils?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Well, you really get sick of coding demos if you have been in the   บ
 บ        demo scene for 10 years doing the same thing.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Rebels is a group that is based in Sweden, does that hinder Rebels  บ
 บ        effectiveness in releasing utils?  After all, European countries    บ
 บ        are supposed to receive computer software a few weeks after the     บ
 บ        United States, or is that not true?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Rebels is no longer based in Sweden since the merge with Pantera,   บ
 บ        over half the group is now based in the US.  Doson and Racjam are   บ
 บ        doing a hell of a job over there.  Comptuer software arrives in     บ
 บ        Europe as fast as it does in the US, so being in Europe does not    บ
 บ        effect the standing of the group.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Does Doson and Racjam help supply for the group, or do they do      บ
 บ        work as the US coordinators of Rebels?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : They have a position that is equal in standing to Omnibuz and I.    บ
 บ        The 4 of us are in charge of Rebels and we all do our bit to help   บ
 บ        the group.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Now that Rebels also has a strong force in the US as well as        บ
 บ        Europe, what do you see for the future of Rebels?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Well, we are all doing this for fun and we are all good friends in  บ
 บ        Rebels.  Lots of the members in Europe are going to the US this     บ
 บ        Autumn.  Since we are such good friends, I guess we will all stick  บ
 บ        together and Rebels will grow bigger and bigger.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned earlier that DOD was going down hill, why do you say  บ
 บ        that is so?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RBS : Well they are not going down hill, it's just that they have not     บ
 บ        released as much in the past weeks as they used to, but every       บ
 บ        group hits a slump every now and then.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      I thought it was pretty cool the day RblChickn walked into            บ
 บ  #Sailormoon and we decided to trade ops, as it were.  I became a member   บ
 บ  of RCN, in charge of channel security, and he got to sit in my channel    บ
 บ  looking cool all night.  While chatting in #RCN one evening, Druggy       บ
 บ  popped in complaining that #Sin had no ops.  After getting ops back for   บ
 บ  the channel twice, we got to talking and I became a member.  About a      บ
 บ  week passed, and things were pretty cool.  I liked working with Druggy,   บ
 บ  and the people in #Sin were real nice.  Soon, however, all hell broke     บ
 บ  loose for a couple of days when Druggy up and went.  He wrote us all,     บ
 บ  saying that he had "lost faith and Sin".  Druggy currently is a part of   บ
 บ  the Motiv8 council, where his fate is being decided.  This interview      บ
 บ  consists of Druggy, the ex-president of Sin (Sinful Traders), and Wildd,  บ
 บ  the new president.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I apologize in advance for the poor quality of my interview with      บ
 บ  Druggy.  During the said interview, both of Motiv8's channels were taken  บ
 บ  over by a friend of mine, no doubt.  While talking to my friend I also    บ
 บ  received a call from my mother, and upon finding out that she was just    บ
 บ  in a car accident I had to leave immediately to pick her up.  Please      บ
 บ  note that I am not taking sides at all.  The following conversation was   บ
 บ  made between Druggy and I :                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When did you first learn about Sin?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : I frist learned about Sin shortly after I left Violation about one  บ
 บ        and a half months ago.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : And you were with it the whole time?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Yes.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Not to suck up or anything, but when I joined, you were a great     บ
 บ        leader of Sin.  You were always busy, always workin hard to keep    บ
 บ        the group going.  You seemed to like it, but then why did you       บ
 บ        start to "lose faith in Sin"?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Well, it goes like this, back in the days of Violation, I worked    บ
 บ        my ass of for the group along with Double E, who later becomes the  บ
 บ        vice president of Sin.  Doublee busted his ass off for the group    บ
 บ        by kicking ass with the uploads, and I would take care of           บ
 บ        organizing and managing the group.  We left Violation mainly        บ
 บ        because everyone was fucking around, and leeching away and so we    บ
 บ        started Sinful Traders.  We were awesome when we were small, but    บ
 บ        when we started to become well known, more people joined, and at    บ
 บ        my fault, I did not put any of the applicants on trial.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : But big groups can make it, you did kick out like 3/4th of them,    บ
 บ        but they all seemed to keep coming back.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Yeah, it was a fucking pain, no one took them off the channel       บ
 บ        bots, and they all still had my email.  Two particular fucks,       บ
 บ        Blankman and Demon of BaC leeched our sites for the good of the     บ
 บ        other group, which really got me pissed.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I made the mistake there.  Nobody had master access on my bots      บ
 บ        except you, Double E, and Wildd.  They couldn't take people off,    บ
 บ        so they kickbanned them until I fixed it.  So basically, you        บ
 บ        decided to just start somewhere else, or did you decide to take     บ
 บ        some of your friends with you to join Motiv8?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Yes, I talked to Mason, and tried to get on one or two of their     บ
 บ        FTP sites so Sin could prosper, so I made him an account on the     บ
 บ        Sin WHQ, and Mason was impressed, so he brought up the idea of a    บ
 บ        merger.  I figured, if I went to Motiv8, I could help them out as   บ
 บ        a council member, I could help organize the group, and I could      บ
 บ        recruit some very dedicated couriers, and I could set up some very  บ
 บ        fast FTP sites.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Ahhh.. so you decided to leave Sin to join Motiv8.  What            บ
 บ        influenced your decision on who you should take along with you to   บ
 บ        Motiv8?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Well, quite simply, people who had their own source of warez.       บ
 บ        Most of the group relied on these few, to get the "stuff" to        บ
 บ        distribute.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did Random end up in jail?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Random is in jail because someone narqed on him.  My guess is that  บ
 บ        someone from Sin who whas furious that I abandoned them.  I gave    บ
 บ        Sin a week trial, they didn't shape up, so I left.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Wildd wasn't so sure that Random was narqed on.  He said that when  บ
 บ        his site got all the uploads from Motiv8, the disk space was        บ
 บ        filled and his administrator found the warez.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : That's a fucking lie.  It was never a MOTIV8 site!  Random was      บ
 บ        working on it!  And some mother fucking ROOT from Canada got his    บ
 บ        ass.  This was Random's second bust within a year.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following conversation was made between Wildd and I :             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How long were you with Sin?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : I've been in Sin since its beginning.  I think it has been 2        บ
 บ        months now.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You were a senior right?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Yes.  Up until now, I was a senior member, but I did more work      บ
 บ        than the job called for.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did you foresee Druggy leaving the group?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : He talked about merging all of Sin into Motiv8, but I had no idea   บ
 บ        that he himself would split.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : He said that in the last 3 weeks or so, too many people joined      บ
 บ        Sin, and it is what screwed up the group.  Do you agree that this   บ
 บ        is one of the reasons the group was having problems?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Well, I don't think the group was ever screwed, other than the      บ
 บ        fact that Druggy started to pay less and less attention to the      บ
 บ        happenings around Sin itself.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did Druggy invite you to go along to Motiv8 with him?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Druggy tried to get me into Motiv8, but I had already expressed my  บ
 บ        strong dislike for Motiv8's workings to many Motiv8 council         บ
 บ        members.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How'd he start to pay less and less attention to Sin?  When I       บ
 บ        joined the group, he was always working hard for us, despite his    บ
 บ        finals.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : He was there, but he put more and more of a work load on seniors,   บ
 บ        and did less and less himself.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Ahh.. well, since I was not a senior, I wouldn't have noticed.  I   บ
 บ        got my fair share of tasks but it wasn't too much in return for     บ
 บ        all I was given.  So you decided you'd want to run Sin?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Ya, I have been with Sin from the beginning, and I looked at it as  บ
 บ        something that I helped shape.  I didn't want to give up on it,     บ
 บ        especially not now, when it needed me most.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you think Sin was hurt badly by Druggy leaving?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : I think Sin was crippled by Druggy leaving, but we were, with the   บ
 บ        dedication of several people (you know who you are), able to        บ
 บ        regroup and come back, stronger than ever.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you don't foresee any problems with Sin in the future?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : The only problem I foresee with Sin in the future is that we need   บ
 บ        more FTP sites to fill.  The couriers are filling hard drive EVERY  บ
 บ        day and they are doing one hell of a job.  I've already had to      บ
 บ        have several of my couriers cut back on their uploading!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So Sin is stronger than ever?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : I think it is.  We went through what should have been a             บ
 บ        devastating time, and came out even better.  I foresee things only  บ
 บ        getting better.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I'm trying to decide if I should join Druggy and a few of the       บ
 บ        others in Motiv8 or stay in Sin.. any advice?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Well.. I think Motiv8 has troubles in the future.  As you saw..     บ
 บ        they are getting hectic there with takeovers and tons of            บ
 บ        idlers/leechers.  There's never any work that gets done in the      บ
 บ        shitty council.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did Sin lose a lot of members to Motiv8 or other groups?  And what  บ
 บ        is going on with Manta's desire to merge Sin with IRC?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Sin lost some people, but none that I miss too much.  We did lose   บ
 บ        many FTP sites.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yeah, I noticed the loss of FTP sites in the last FTP site list I   บ
 บ        got.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Do you know anything about Random being in jail?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Druggy mentioned that.  I need to talk to him about it.  Manta is   บ
 บ        a traitor.  He came into Sin, and said that I announced we were     บ
 บ        merging with IRC when I was away.  Fortunately, because of a few    บ
 บ        people's quick work, I was able to keep ALL members from leaving    บ
 บ        for IRC.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Yeah, I was there.  He said that you would be OK with it, but did   บ
 บ        not say that you would agree.  I was talking to Crash and a few     บ
 บ        others and they all said that you would give a flat out "NO" to     บ
 บ        the merge.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Random was put in jail because this was the second time he got      บ
 บ        caught.  It was not that anyone neccesarily narqed, but that the    บ
 บ        system administrators caught on when the increased Motiv8           บ
 บ        uploading kicked in, and the space dwindled.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Yeah, Druggy said that Random's boss emailed him and told him to    บ
 บ        fuck off.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Ya.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WLD : Motiv8 has lost a lot of FTP sites it seems.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Despite the desires of Manta, Sin will merge with no one.  The      บ
 บ        dedication of our people have made the Sin name as big as ever,     บ
 บ        and they deserve to keep that name.  I won't let anyone take it     บ
 บ        over.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Endeavour            บ
 บ    Subject  : COPS Doing Shareware???   Affiliation : COPS Founder         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I've seen COPS (Couriers of Pirated Software) release both games    บ
 บ        and utils here and there, why has COPS not taken the move to        บ
 บ        specialize in one field of releasing, or has it already done so?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS now specializes in utils only.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why have you decided to do so?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well, I feel that if a group releases anything that it can get its  บ
 บ        hands on, it's really not a very professional group.  But if you    บ
 บ        release within a certain specialized area, such as utils, then it   บ
 บ        makes the group seem more "professional".  Another advantage of     บ
 บ        only releasing utils is that I will be able to trade games for      บ
 บ        utils with other groups, which would help make for good relations   บ
 บ        with the rest of the scene.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So COPS trades it's games with other games groups?  Has COPS        บ
 บ        traded games for utils with other games groups yet?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well COPS hasn't exactly traded ANY games yet with any groups, but  บ
 บ        we plan on trading games with other groups in the future if we get  บ
 บ        a hold of some hot game releases.  I plan to trade games for utils  บ
 บ        with groups such as ROR (Release on Rampage) and Napalm.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Just a few weeks ago, I saw that COPS released Blake Stone :        บ
 บ        Aliens of Gold, the files dated back to 1993, about the same time   บ
 บ        Wolfenstein was first released to the public, why would groups      บ
 บ        such as ROR and Napalm want to trade their utils with games by      บ
 บ        COPS which have a reputation of low quality?  Anyhow, ROR has       บ
 บ        already promised to trade its utils and games strictly with         บ
 บ        Mortality and not with COPS?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, I remember that release of Blake Stone : Aliens of Gold.       บ
 บ        That was a BAD release and COPS apologizes for that, but we don't   บ
 บ        intend to release anything like that in the future.  It was a bad   บ
 บ        call on my part.  Well, if ROR has already made a decision on       บ
 บ        trading utils for games only with Mortality, then that's fine.  I   บ
 บ        will find another group such as Napalm, and if COPS can't find any  บ
 บ        other groups, then fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) will be our    บ
 บ        next candidate.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Most Napalm suppliers are also in grousp such as DOD (Drink or      บ
 บ        Die) and PWA (Pirates with Attitudes), and thus have to supply for  บ
 บ        those groups, so saying that Napalm will help supply utils for      บ
 บ        COPS is definitely out of the question.  On the note of fATE, why   บ
 บ        would you trade releases with fATE?  fATE is a courier group, is    บ
 บ        it not?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Like I said, I will find some other groups to trade releases with   บ
 บ        after consulting with my council.  Those just happened to be the 2  บ
 บ        groups that I could name off the top of my head.  fATE is official  บ
 บ        couriers for COPS, and fATE does have a releasing section.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of COPS best releases in the recent weeks?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS has released great software such as Visual Object COBOL for    บ
 บ        Windows 95/NT Beta 3 and WebManager for Win95 Beta v.1.1.3.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why are those releases all beta, would it be that COPS has          บ
 บ        suppliers that work for those companies?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : You can say that.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : As an editor of RCN, I try to keep an unbiased opinion toward       บ
 บ        groups.  However, wherever I go, it seems to me that there is a     บ
 บ        general consensus among to scene to look upon COPS as a really      บ
 บ        "lame" group.  The scene accuses COPS of releasing nothing but      บ
 บ        dupes and shareware, why do you think that is so?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Haha, well, as I learned from the latest issue of RCN (and I whole  บ
 บ        heartedly agree), is that if you call someone "lame", that person   บ
 บ        who call people lame is the person that is really lame.  But, to    บ
 บ        tell you the truth, we have only released 1 dupe and we have yet    บ
 บ        to anything that can be considered shareware. I don't know where    บ
 บ        they would get the idea that we release in those two categories,    บ
 บ        because every group has their share of "dupes" but COPS has had     บ
 บ        only 1, and the scene should give us credit on that.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're saying that COPS has never released any shareware or      บ
 บ        freeware, and that COPS has only duped once in its entire           บ
 บ        existence?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, COPS has only duped once, and COPS has never released          บ
 บ        shareware or freeware.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you lie often?  Anyway, COPS is very fortunate to have fATE as   บ
 บ        its official couriers, how did you acquire such a good standing     บ
 บ        and respectable courier group to become officials with COPS?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well, MALiCE used to be official couriers for COPS, but then        บ
 บ        MALiCE kicked COPS out, but before that happened, Doobie from fATE  บ
 บ        was in close contact with me, and when MALiCE kicked COPS out, I    บ
 บ        jumped on the chance to get fATE in as COPS' official couriers.     บ
 บ        fATE has been doing a lot more than some of the courier groups      บ
 บ        around, especially MALiCE, which I think is DEAD now.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did MALiCE kick COPS out as official couriers?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : The reason MALiCE kicked out COPS was because the council members   บ
 บ        in MALiCE were REALLY poor with their members.  There were fights   บ
 บ        within the group all the time.  I had repeatedly asked them to      บ
 บ        support the COPS FTP sites, they merely ignored me.  I got sick of  บ
 บ        MALiCE and the MALiCE members got sick of the council and left.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you see for the future of COPS?  Do you see it becoming     บ
 บ        one of the strong utils groups in the future?  There's a quote      บ
 บ        found in the COPS NFO, which goes as follows "Keep an eye on us,    บ
 บ        cuz we are coming very strong, VERY strong, and we are ready to     บ
 บ        tear it up and take all."  Do you believe that COPS is indeed       บ
 บ        becoming very strong, VERY strong?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, I think so.  I think that COPS will become VERY strong.  It    บ
 บ        may take a couple of years, but I think that sooner or later, we    บ
 บ        will be as good as groups such as DOD and PWA.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Don't you think that aspiring to be as good as DOD and PWA might    บ
 บ        be impossible for a group such as COPS?  After all, most people in  บ
 บ        the scene are very stubborn, and most already have their heart set  บ
 บ        to believing that COPS is very lame and only releases freeware and  บ
 บ        shareware even when that might not be the case.  Perhaps, it would  บ
 บ        be easier for you to just kill COPS, and start a totally new        บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Hehe, like how you did to Legacy?  I doubt it.  Maybe it will be    บ
 บ        impossible, but I am sure that we will have "some" impact on the    บ
 บ        scene.  When people COPS releases in the future, I am sure they     บ
 บ        will come to change their minds.  But then again, you never know    บ
 บ        what will happen in the future.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, that is true, but history does repeat itself.  Anyway,         บ
 บ        according to my sources, you also ran an e-mag called Horizons,     บ
 บ        what happened to it?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, we were, but a lot of our Horizon writers weren't committed    บ
 บ        enough and soon, the group died off.  I see no reason to publish    บ
 บ        an e-mag if RCN is in the scene.  I think that you guys are the     บ
 บ        best and that there should be no other e-mag.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I must admire your tenacity in running COPS, if I were running      บ
 บ        COPS, I would have killed it off long ago, but you seem to be a     บ
 บ        hard worker, what's your secret?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS may not be the best group around, but we are sure as hell      บ
 บ        trying to contribute whatever we can to the scene.  And even        บ
 บ        though we may not have the "best" people in our group, or "known"   บ
 บ        people, there are a lot of new prospective members out their that   บ
 บ        are willing to commit time and energy into a group, even if that    บ
 บ        group may not be as good as DOD or PWA.  When you come into our     บ
 บ        IRC channel #C.O.P.S., you would hardly recognize anyone there.     บ
 บ        That's because these members are the NEW batch of people coming     บ
 บ        into the scene.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Chuck McGinnes                                                บ
 บ    Subject : Teen Charged With Hacking FAU computer                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BOCA RATON - a recently graduated high school senior has been         บ
 บ  charged with breaking into the computer system at Florida Atlantic State  บ
 บ  University's College of Science and Engineering, destroying a             บ
 บ  professor's electronic mail and transferring files to the internet.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thomas Robert Stromberg, 18, who just graduted from Olympic Heights   บ
 บ  High School, was arrested Thursday at his home west of Boca Raton.  He    บ
 บ  was charged with two felonies - offenses against intellectual property    บ
 บ  and offenses against computer users.  Investigators from the FDLE         บ
 บ  (Florida Department of Law Enforcement) and FAU seized a computer and     บ
 บ  related equipment and material from Stromberg's home at 9596 Lancaster    บ
 บ  Place.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      FDLE agents also seized computers from other homes in the Boca Raton  บ
 บ  area.  Additional arrests are expected, FAU Detective Carl "Chuck" Aurin  บ
 บ  said.  The investigation began in February after Elise Angiollilo, FAU's  บ
 บ  director of tele-communications, discovered someone had gained access to  บ
 บ  the computers in the science and engineering department.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The hackers apparently used the account of a former FAU student to    บ
 บ  get into the unversity's computer system.  Once they had access, they     บ
 บ  twice tried to crash the computer system and wiped out the electronic     บ
 บ  mail system of Mahesh Neelakanta, the department's computer system        บ
 บ  coordinator.  Information and copyrighted software from the computer      บ
 บ  files were transferred to the Internet, where the data could be copied    บ
 บ  by anyone using the Internet.  FAU officials would not say what was in    บ
 บ  the files.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "The university has very significant information in the computer.     บ
 บ  The equipment is used by the state for a specific purpose : education     บ
 บ  and research," said Tom Horton, a computer science and engineering        บ
 บ  professor.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Neelakanta found and FAU computer account that was being used to      บ
 บ  request information from an outside computer system.  The outside system  บ
 บ  asked for personal information and the individual using the account       บ
 บ  entered Stromberg's name, according to an arrest report.  Stromberg told  บ
 บ  the police he used a program to crack password files that allowed him     บ
 บ  into several user accounts where he stored pirated software.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is not the first time hackers have broken into the computer      บ
 บ  system of a government agency in Palm Beach County.  In 1992, a           บ
 บ  15-year-old Jupiter boy allegedely tinkered his way into a South Florida  บ
 บ  Water Management District computer system.  Sheryl Woodm a district       บ
 บ  attorney, said she could not recall if criminal charges were filed        บ
 บ  against the boy, but she remembered seeing a letter of apology from the   บ
 บ  youth.  Investigators said most hackers break into computer systems for   บ
 บ  the bragging rights.  They usually write bulletin boards and share the    บ
 บ  information they obtain with other hackers.  Stromberg, who was a member  บ
 บ  of his school's computer club, went by the name Dr. Jekyll.  He is being  บ
 บ  held at the county jail on $1,000 bail.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Kysr Soze                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Demaxxus *BUSTED*!!!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm a close personal friend of Demaxxus, and this morning (Monday,    บ
 บ  June 3rd), I called him at about 8:50am, like I usually do (to make sure  บ
 บ  he's awake), but this time our call was a little bit different.  There    บ
 บ  was no, "Oh ya, I'm on my way, I'll meet you there."  Instead, his reply  บ
 บ  was "No, I'm not going to school today, and mabe not for a while."        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On monday, June 3rd, at approximately 7:30am, the house of Demaxxus,  บ
 บ  Nabiki Tendo, was raided.  The RCMP (Royal Canadian Mounted Police) was   บ
 บ  looking for miscellaneous computer peripherals and accessories that were  บ
 บ  shoplifted from stores such as Future Shop, Business Depot, and Walmart.  บ
 บ  They were also searching for computer components that were apparently     บ
 บ  missing from the school in which he attended.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The RCMP didn't find what they were looking for (like Demaxxus would  บ
 บ  be dumb enough to keep stolen stuff around), but they did confiscate an   บ
 บ  IBM Thinkpad, two 486 Dx/66s, hundreds of disks, numberous modems         บ
 บ  (ranging from 14.4 to 28.8), along with a bunch of other computer         บ
 บ  equipment.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, along with the thefts, they revealed that they were watching    บ
 บ  him for some time now and had been tracing his calls.  They realized      บ
 บ  that he had been using stolen calling/credit cards to call long distance  บ
 บ  and order computer accessories.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I personally think that it's really shitty that he got busted,        บ
 บ  because over the past few months, besides occasionally giving a release   บ
 บ  to a group, he had been trying to give up the illigal shit.  He left      บ
 บ  such groups as as ROR (Release on Rampage), Pantera, KTF, Demoltion, and  บ
 บ  started joining groups like FSW, Punc, and ACiDiC, so he could code       บ
 บ  instead of supplying warez.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, for all of you out there that knew Demaxxus, write a few words  บ
 บ  for him, and send them to RCN, or email them to him.  Or if you see me    บ
 บ  on IRC, I'm online as Kysr_Soze, send them to me, he's gonna be kinda     บ
 บ  bored now, and he'll need something to read.  Oh ya, and if you were      บ
 บ  expecting an ascii or a ppe from him, i hope there's no hurry...          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Yeah!  He gave me his Internet account :).  Sorry, had to be done,   บ
 บ       needed something to un-depress myself.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Marb0l                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : What Happened to DOD?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My name is Marb0l and I am writing due to the fact that many people   บ
 บ  don't really know what happend to DOD (Drink or Die).  I want to clear    บ
 บ  things up.  First off, let me say where I stand in this issue.  I am      บ
 บ  currently NOT part of DOD and never was.  I'm just a good friend of a     บ
 บ  couple of DOD members who I have acquired meeting logs from.  Anyways,    บ
 บ  this is basically what led to the DOD downfall.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Around 6 months ago, a PWA (Pirates with Attitudes) and Razor 1911    บ
 บ  supplier we will call BILL was intending on moving to DOD from PWA, but   บ
 บ  as you all know, DOD and PWA have good relations, so the DOD council      บ
 บ  objected.  Then BILL approached The Speed Racer which is good buds with   บ
 บ  Jimmy Jamez regarding this matter.  Jimmy Jamez finally accepted BILL     บ
 บ  into DOD.  As soon as PWA heard about this, they went into a craze and    บ
 บ  started to confront DOD and at this point, Jimmy Jamez was already out    บ
 บ  of the scene so it was all up to the council to direct.  Things really    บ
 บ  heated up when the DOD council said they had no clue what was going on.   บ
 บ  PWA didn't believe them so they raged against DOD.  After a couple of     บ
 บ  days, the council notified Quackers (DOD Council, good ties with PWA).    บ
 บ  He came and after some time, cleared things up.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Months passed and a certain DOD member was kicked from the group.     บ
 บ  He believed that he was kicked for a childish reason so he went to talk   บ
 บ  to some DOD and PWA suppliers to steal them and create his own group.     บ
 บ  Believe it or not, some agreed and then eventually DOD found out.  They   บ
 บ  contacted PWA and decided to talk to Quackers to come again and clear     บ
 บ  things up.  In Quacker's eyes, he was pissed and did kind of get things   บ
 บ  settled but then he came up with the idea to merge DOD and PWA into one   บ
 บ  group, keeping the name PWA.  DOD, of course, was not too happy with      บ
 บ  this because Quackers announced it in the meeting that he had told some   บ
 บ  suppliers not to do anything for personal reasons and also that PWA was   บ
 บ  not giving DOD a fair deal.  Still, he wanted things to happen but DOD    บ
 บ  decided against it and so Quackers LEFT DOD.  He also took DOD's top 3    บ
 บ  suppliers with him.  From there, DOD lost others as we know now such as   บ
 บ  Egoistic Fate, their WHQ, suppliers, and also Analog Kid.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In my view, this showed that Quackers screwed DOD and wanted to       บ
 บ  totally get away from this.  After this, I really don't think DOD will    บ
 บ  be the same unless Quackers decides to give the suppliers back which I    บ
 บ  don't think will ever happen.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Good Job Prestige!                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few months ago, the scene was presented with a new group,           บ
 บ  Prestige.  It started out just like any other group, kind of like COPS    บ
 บ  is right now, a bit lame, but they tried, and they tried hard, and        บ
 บ  something great became of their work.  I remember when they released      บ
 บ  Virtual Pool for Windows 3.1 on the same day that Napalm released the     บ
 บ  Windows 95 version.  That didn't work too well for them.  Little things   บ
 บ  like that made us think of Prestige as "just another group".  However,    บ
 บ  their perseverance has pulled them through those hard times and now they  บ
 บ  have pushed their way to being the #1 games group in the scene.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Somewhat unbelievable, and a bit mind boggling, that even when it     บ
 บ  was small, Prestige managed to get many Hybrid, Dynamix, and Razor 1911   บ
 บ  members to join it.  Within a week of their unification into Prestige,    บ
 บ  these members watched it go up in ranking.  Battle Arena : Toshinden,     บ
 บ  Settlers II, Total Mayhem, and Strife are just a number of this group's   บ
 บ  recent releases, and quality shines through their names.  It is a true    บ
 บ  challenge to create a group that releases with such great quality.  The   บ
 บ  pressures of the scene today make it hard to pass any release.  It is     บ
 บ  then an even harder challenge to release quality before some other group  บ
 บ  like Razor 1911 or Hybrid gets to it.  Then, the challenge toughens even  บ
 บ  more when the group is expected to do this on a regular basis (3-5        บ
 บ  releases a week!).                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Of course, with such greatness come a few mistakes, especially in a   บ
 บ  young group like Prestige.  A recent example of this would be Earthworm   บ
 บ  Jim II, in which they left out DOS4GW.EXE (another group promptly         บ
 บ  released a fix).  I don't expect to see too many more blunt mistakes      บ
 บ  such as this one in the future, though, Prestige will undoubtedly learn   บ
 บ  from its mistakes.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am still confused as to how Prestige managed to gather so many of   บ
 บ  the scene's greats into a relatively young group.  Perhaps they just      บ
 บ  needed a change of mood.  When one joins a new group, he generally gets   บ
 บ  a feeling of motivation to make that group the greatest, and I would      บ
 บ  assume that it is for this reason that they all joined.  Either that, or  บ
 บ  the Prestige leaders have REALLY high charisma!                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Prestige has a big future ahead of it, and I have no doubt in my      บ
 บ  mind that they will achieve their highest goals in due time.  However,    บ
 บ  there is something they must remember.  In the scene, you get nowhere     บ
 บ  with a big ego.  As we saw last week in RCN #16, The Renegade Chemist, a  บ
 บ  Prestige member, thought he was "a god".  Such feelings will get you and  บ
 บ  your group nowhere, and it would be a shame for such a great group to     บ
 บ  end up crumbling because of things like this.  The Renegade Chemist       บ
 บ  originally left Razor 1911 due to a conflict involving his ego between    บ
 บ  him and The Speed Racer.  He then joined Hybrid, and ultimately left      บ
 บ  that as well due to the same problem.  Finally, he joined Dynamix, and    บ
 บ  yes, you guessed it, left that due to a problem with his ego as well.     บ
 บ  Is this a flashing yellow light?  Does this mean something about what is  บ
 บ  to come?  Perhaps, perhaps not, but it has been proven that his ego       บ
 บ  hasn't helped him any, and it would be a shame if it struck again.        บ
 บ  Assuming that his ego problem does effect his standing in the Prestige,   บ
 บ  he might leave it too.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So the competition that Razor 1911 and Hybrid desired is here, and,   บ
 บ  well, you've got to wonder if they didn't like it better before, when     บ
 บ  they could manage to get more than 2 releases a week!  Great work         บ
 บ  Prestige, you guys are doing an awesome job, keep up the good work!  And  บ
 บ  a word for Razor 1911 and Hybrid, you're the greatest, you can make it    บ
 บ  through this!  Push your weight around a bit, show Prestige what you're   บ
 บ  really made of!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Lost Soul                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Crackers, the Brains of the Scene                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hi everybody, I'm Lost Soul, a cracker.  Many of you have probably    บ
 บ  noticed some games and utilities that I have cracked.  I cracked          บ
 บ  Napalm's recent release of Tony La Russa 3 Baseball 1996 Edition.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In this article, I'll talk about cracking in general and about a      บ
 บ  cracker's life.  My article is directed to the warez scene, the one       บ
 บ  which deals with the Internet and IRC as it's main field of activity.  A  บ
 บ  work as crackers isn't a matter of trickery or agility of hands, we are   บ
 บ  the most quality force of the scene.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We deserve RESPECT, our work is the hardest work in the scene, the    บ
 บ  fact the most of us can crack anything within 10 minutes doesn't make     บ
 บ  cracking easier.  Cracking is an intellectual challenge, cracking takes   บ
 บ  a lot of reasoning and research work, every crack is different from one   บ
 บ  another.  Not all the dongles are the same, neither are the cd-checks, a  บ
 บ  working keymaker might take up to 2 hours, 2 boring hours that you sit    บ
 บ  in front of the computer in text mode and try to understand something     บ
 บ  that you're not supposed to understand, then, you have to break through   บ
 บ  it...                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WITHOUT CRACKERS, MOST GROUPS WOULD DIE OR THEY WOULD ONLY BE RELEASING   บ
 บ  NONWORKING SHIT.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Some words about benefits, YEZ!  Cracking is also the easiest way to  บ
 บ  get leech account on great sites, if you're a good cracker that can       บ
 บ  handle all kinds of protection and can also make a fully-working-crack    บ
 บ  fast, then you'll find your place in a quality group that have quality    บ
 บ  sites, very soon (2 to 6 months).                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVERY LAMER CAN BE COURIER, BUT YOU CANNOT REPLACE A CRACKER.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      No more need to do the boring job of uploading and downloading to     บ
 บ  and from BBSes, and/or FTP sites, there's no need to type 'ls' on an FTP  บ
 บ  site prompt every 180 seconds.  There's no need to open multiple FTP      บ
 บ  windows at once, nor is there any more need to leech utilities and games  บ
 บ  that you'll never use.  Once you have your FTP site in your hand, you're  บ
 บ  free to leech away as much as you need.  More than it, you can sell your  บ
 บ  FTP sites to people (that you know and trust) and even earn money!!!      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  WITHOUT PAYING A CRACKER WITH LEECH ACCOUNTS, A CRACKER WILL SIMPLY QUIT  บ
 บ  FOR ANOTHER GROUP THAT OFFERS MORE.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Some words about fame, crackers always win some fame.  If you crack   บ
 บ  for utilities group such as UCF (United Cracking Force, for those of you  บ
 บ  who live too deep in the scene) every damn lamer around the world will    บ
 บ  remember your name.  Everybody uses UCF's wonderful keymakers and cracks  บ
 บ  such as Terminate, Bluewave, CU See-Me, WebEdit, hot dog, etc.  Once      บ
 บ  you're good enough to join UCF (UCF isn't accepting new members), your    บ
 บ  name shall remain a legend, no one actually remembers who cracked DOD or  บ
 บ  PWA's latest quality $10,000 ware that needs a 586-120Mhz + 32 MB RAM,    บ
 บ  but everyone will remember the cracker of A USEFUL PROGRAM.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH <sigh>, THE GOOD LIFE OF BEING A CRACKER???            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Life in utilities groups are the best, you hardly crack there, you    บ
 บ  crack maximum 2 programs per 3 weeks, most of the time you can sit in     บ
 บ  amenity and enjoy your leech accounts, this time, you don't have to       บ
 บ  upload to ANYONE.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you crack for groups such as DOD or PWA, you'll win a lot of       บ
 บ  respect from the end of the user to the end of the leaders, you'll get    บ
 บ  1-3 offers every week to leave your current group for another.  A lot of  บ
 บ  leaders will attempt to steal you from your current group into their      บ
 บ  group, they'll promise you better/more sites and calling cards and as     บ
 บ  much as you need!                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LIFE IN GAMES GROUPS                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you join a games group, you'll always be in tension, you'll have   บ
 บ  to face some of the most weird protection you've ever seen.  Utilities    บ
 บ  that you usually use to crack programs wont work, you'll have to be more  บ
 บ  brilliant for it (BPINT in win / 4GW cracking) you'll crack 1-4 games     บ
 บ  every week, most have weird protection as mentioned above you'll get      บ
 บ  voice phone calls in the middle of the night.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SOOOOOOOOOO, I WANT TO LIVE THE GOOD LIFE, HOW DO I BECOME A CRACKER?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Don't assume that anyone can be a cracker, on your way climbing to    บ
 บ  the top, you'll face many difficulties, as mentioned before, "cracking    บ
 บ  takes a lot of reasoning and research work".  If you're not good in math  บ
 บ  or have low IQ, there's a high possibility that you simply don't match    บ
 บ  this job, so don't even bother to try.  A few of the crackers I know are  บ
 บ  gifted.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a cracker, you must first get yourself a book on assembly,  บ
 บ  and you must then know it inside out.  Then, you must get yourself the    บ
 บ  needed tools (Soft-Ice DOS/WIN/WIN95 and Hacker's View).  Then, you must  บ
 บ  get yourself shareware utilities to crack to gain more experience.  If    บ
 บ  you did all this, you should be smart enough to know all the rest.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Never stick to the NOP crack, this one is the safest way to become   บ
 บ       a lame cracker.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
