 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Warez Man                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Cable Modems                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most serious couriers or suppliers have probably heard about cable    บ
 บ  modem technology by now, and a select few might even know some details    บ
 บ  about them.  A very fortunate bunch are even using them as I speak.       บ
 บ  Cable modems are devices that modulate data into RF frequencies that may  บ
 บ  be transmitted over coaxial cable (RG-6 1GHz for you info maniacs).  The  บ
 บ  signal is then converted at the curb to light impulses which travel over  บ
 บ  fiber optic cable to the headend (usually cable company's headquarters).  บ
 บ  Then it is fed into a frequency translator ($2995, owned by the cable     บ
 บ  company), which serves as the focal point of the system by routing data   บ
 บ  traffic from the reverse channel (anywhere from 11.75 to 541.25 MHz) to   บ
 บ  the forward channel (at least 10 KHz away from input frequency) for       บ
 บ  broadcast to the network devices.  The common cable modem, the Zenith     บ
 บ  Network Device, is currently :                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ          Zenith HOMEWorks           500 Kilo Bits/Second     $395          บ
 บ          Zenith HOMEWorks             4 Mega Bits/Second     $395          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The previous 2 use an included ISA Ethernet card (this card is        บ
 บ  provided by Zenith, and is proprietary, it can not be exchanged with any  บ
 บ  other card).                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ          Zenith HOMEWorks Universal 500 Kilo Bits/Second     $495          บ
 บ          Zenith HOMEWorks Universal   4 Mega Bits/Second     $495          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Universals all have conversion hardware built in (which accounts  บ
 บ  for the increased size) and have a RJ-45 (10-Base-T) port which will      บ
 บ  connect to any Ethernet card with 10-Base-T, allowing it to work on any   บ
 บ  OS that supports networking.  They are available in dual Ethernet port    บ
 บ  models for $550.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ          Zenith ChannelMizer/SNMP   500 Kilo Bits/Second     $995          บ
 บ          Zenith ChannelMizer/SNMP     4 Mega Bits/Second     $995          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The ChannelMizers provide Ethernet service connectivity.  Including   บ
 บ  2 AUI (DTE) connectors and 1 AUI (DCE) connection, these are suited for   บ
 บ  connection to a hub for distribution to an entire network.  The computer  บ
 บ  applications of the future (i.e. real-time video) will require multiple   บ
 บ  ultra-high-speed delivery channels to support the anticipated demand.     บ
 บ  These channels will deliver data at rates at or near 40 Mbps using VBS    บ
 บ  (or QAM) modulation.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With this type of architecture, a high-speed data communications      บ
 บ  link is provided for a variety of applications including Internet         บ
 บ  access, distance learning, work-at-home, healthcare, business to          บ
 บ  business and community services.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This technology, combined with low pricing ($25 to $50 per month for  บ
 บ  500K) will allow people in the warez scene to have high speed             บ
 บ  connections at home, not just at the office.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I believe that this and DVD technology (covered in Issue #15 of RCN)  บ
 บ  will drastically change our scene's productivity.  Being able to get one  บ
 บ  CD or even many CDs in the time it would currently take to download a     บ
 บ  normal 10 disk release, and then putting it on an 4.7 gig data cartridge  บ
 บ  will definitely surpass the old analog clunkiness of 28.8's and hard      บ
 บ  drives.  Actually having modems that are faster than our hard drives      บ
 บ  will definitely be a thing to put a smile on your face.  We've all had    บ
 บ  to sit through long downloads, just to find that the release doesn't      บ
 บ  work.  However, cable modem technology will cause much confusion as soon  บ
 บ  as it is first introduced.  The reason for this is that the Internet      บ
 บ  backbone is not currently capable of pushing 500+ kbps to each and every  บ
 บ  user that is online at any given modem.  But as always, the Internet      บ
 บ  backbone is constantly being upgraded, and some time in the future, we    บ
 บ  can all expect to be able to download a disk every 3 seconds. This        บ
 บ  technology is one that can only improve the standing of the scene and     บ
 บ  the way in which it works.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Conway                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : 300,000 Very Happy People                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As many of you already know, there is such a thing called AOL.        บ
 บ  Yeah, you say, it's the lamest collection of 5 million people             บ
 บ  imaginable!  Well, let's look at this from a fresh standpoint.  Out of    บ
 บ  AOL's 5 million members, 4.7 million are your average Joe who just think  บ
 บ  it's "cool" that someone can "e-mail" them, and that they are on the      บ
 บ  "Information Superhighway", (God, I hate that term!) but what about the   บ
 บ  other 300,000 people?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What about the ones that hang out in AOL's "warez" chat rooms?  This  บ
 บ  can be broken down like this : 85% are total lamers who can't get into    บ
 บ  the shittiest pirate board, 15% are people who don't have time to call    บ
 บ  regular pirate boards and don't have high-speed Internet connections.     บ
 บ  Even with these seemingly unfavorable percentages, the "elite" of AOL     บ
 บ  have managed to courier huge amounts of warez and distribute them to      บ
 บ  many more people than plausible via FTP or DCC.  This is because getting  บ
 บ  warez from one place to another using the AOL mailing system does not     บ
 บ  require the actual transfer of data.  Only the references to the files    บ
 บ  are assigned to users.  Therefore, it makes it possible to transfer       บ
 บ  gigabytes in minutes (i.e. average size of a file attached to an e-mail   บ
 บ  is 10-20 megs, massmail of 100 messages takes about 3 minutes - 1 gig).   บ
 บ  On the base of this relatively high speed infrastructure, it is much      บ
 บ  easier to courier warez.  Considering this ease-of-transfer, and          บ
 บ  relative ease-of-use of AOL in general, dozens of groups form and die in  บ
 บ  months on AOL.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most of them are victims of the mile-high egos of their leaders and   บ
 บ  members, or just plain laziness.  But some of them survive, and deliver   บ
 บ  quality releases from groups like Hybrid, Napalm, Razor 1911, and more.   บ
 บ  One example is UPS - the frontier group on AOL.  The "couriering" nature  บ
 บ  of AOL makes it a bad base for releasing groups, so the only groups       บ
 บ  found on AOL are ones that courier.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since the idea of the scene is to make good software accessible to    บ
 บ  all for evaluation, AOL could be said to provide a good extension of the  บ
 บ  scene and its purpose.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฿ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Digitex                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Groups.. Time Consuming?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Many have, in the past, asked me what it takes to start a release     บ
 บ  group.  Unfortunately, most asked me before I had ever considered         บ
 บ  starting one.  I would always just say "I have no idea, it's too time     บ
 บ  consuming", or something to that effect.  But in truth, I have found      บ
 บ  that it has several advantages over starting a courier group.  Here's a   บ
 บ  general tutorial as to how to one can get a release group going and also  บ
 บ  how to keep it going, provided you eventually learn what you're doing     บ
 บ  and keep that up.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First, you must be ready to sit around sometimes doing all-nighters   บ
 บ  working on a release.  You must be able to stay on IRC all night          บ
 บ  chatting about one particular release if it is required that you do so.   บ
 บ  You must also be very perceptive if you are the one checking the          บ
 บ  releases, to make sure that the release has no bugs or such things like   บ
 บ  copy protection or cd checks that might have been overlooked by the       บ
 บ  cracker.  You could do what Hybrid and probably a few other groups do     บ
 บ  and just decompile the code and add your own special little effects, or   บ
 บ  you could just crack it plain and simple.  Whatever you do, though, make  บ
 บ  sure you have more than one person check the program.  Nobody's perfect,  บ
 บ  especially not after having been on IRC all night.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Next, you have to either be a very good negotiator or you just have   บ
 บ  to know a lot of different people.  You're not going to be able to do     บ
 บ  everything by yourself, even if you think you can.  There's a lot of      บ
 บ  individual work that needs to be done to get a release group going.  You  บ
 บ  have to have a cracker, packager, and supplier just to get one release    บ
 บ  out.  You should have more than one of all of those, in case one of them  บ
 บ  isn't around to help, so you can get the release out as quickly as        บ
 บ  possible, without compromising quality.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It is important to have a lot of quantity in your releases, but it    บ
 บ  is equally important to have quality, if not more so.  If you release 15  บ
 บ  games a month and none of them work, nobody is going to want to have      บ
 บ  anything to do with you and then even if you do start releasing working   บ
 บ  programs, your reputation will be so bad that nobody will download        บ
 บ  anything of yours.  That's one main reason you want to have more than     บ
 บ  one person look at the release before it gets out onto the Internet, and  บ
 บ  then around the world.  You definitely don't want to turn into an early   บ
 บ  Napalm, releasing the program and THEN a fix for it!                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Make sure you can get an official courier group, or have internal     บ
 บ  couriers to spread the warez for you, but preferably an official          บ
 บ  courier, because you don't want to have so many members that you forget   บ
 บ  who is in the group.  Still, you don't want so few people that everybody  บ
 บ  has to work their ass off for every single release.  They probably have   บ
 บ  a life too, unless they happen to be Endeavour of COPS (Couriers of       บ
 บ  Pirated Software) or tKLP of ROR (Release on Rampage).                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You might try a PPE division, but I haven't really seen many groups   บ
 บ  actually release any QUALITY PPEs.  Most are just recompiled versions of  บ
 บ  old PPEs.  Try splitting the group into many divisions, getting one or    บ
 บ  two people dedicated to monitoring what's going on in their area, things  บ
 บ  will go much smoother that way.  If some area seems to be lacking things  บ
 บ  to do, and another area has many people doing nothing, get those idling   บ
 บ  people into the other area, perhaps they will actually help.  And you     บ
 บ  don't necessarily have to have mercy on slackers, they don't deserve to   บ
 บ  be in your group if they can't contribute.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another important factor to a group is its BBSes.  You could either   บ
 บ  have them or just disregard the idea of having BBSes all together.        บ
 บ  BBSes aren't entirely useful, since the whole scene operates on the       บ
 บ  Internet these days, but maybe you want to have them just to give your    บ
 บ  couriers something else to do, to get rid of the tension of the           บ
 บ  Internet, and it also gives an extra section to add to your NFO!          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Art?  Who cares about art?!  Maybe somebody does.  If your NFO file   บ
 บ  looks like it should be titled "Revenge of TheDraw Fonts", you probably   บ
 บ  won't have such a great impression on people.  This goes for your DIZ as  บ
 บ  well.  You might also want to setup a web page one of these days, and if  บ
 บ  you have all kinds of neat pictures for them to look at, it's going to    บ
 บ  be more interesting and catch people's attention more easily.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You should try and get everything going as soon as possible, and see  บ
 บ  that the members of your group are as dedicated as possible.  Many        บ
 บ  groups do not allow their members to be in another group, but many do to  บ
 บ  give their members experience.  Try to get as many experienced members    บ
 บ  as possible, but you don't want to have an experienced member who is in   บ
 บ  38 different groups.  He probably won't be able to give his most to all   บ
 บ  the groups, and definitely will give most of his releases to other        บ
 บ  groups, and that may not do much other than add another name to your      บ
 บ  NFO.                                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/16/96 -> 05/22/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ

 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ

 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/23/96 -> 05/29/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/09/96 -> 05/15/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/16/96 -> 05/22/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -Rating scale:                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ         (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                             บ
 บ        (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                       บ
 บ        (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                           บ
 บ        (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.       บ
 บ        (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.             บ
 บ        (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.         บ
 บ        (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                      บ
 บ            100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in `ity'.  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow nfo directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just because it     บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                       -<*><*> THE GAME REVIEW <*><*>-                      บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  DEATHKEEP (c) SSI                     [xx/34]                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I had a bit of a problem getting this to install, kept getting        บ
 บ  'script error in line 197'.  If anyone else has this problem, go into     บ
 บ  the install dir, edit dk.inf, and find the line 'Directory [SOURCE DIR]   บ
 บ  := DK'.  Change DK to "." then save it, and it should install fine.       บ
 บ  When playing, it keeps coming up with some sound error, if someone works  บ
 บ  out how to stop this, please let me (_lunatic on IRC) know.  You have a   บ
 บ  choice of three pre-generated characters, which pissed me off (how hard   บ
 บ  would it have been to let you create your own character?), but you do     บ
 บ  get a nice animated intro once you've chosen one.  The game itself looks  บ
 บ  quite nice, til you start moving.  Damn thing moves far too fast, turns   บ
 บ  too fast, and generally makes it damn hard to play.  Playing the dwarf,   บ
 บ  I found an axe and chainmail right near the start, but couldn't work out  บ
 บ  how to put the chainmail on for ages.  The inventory screen shows up      บ
 บ  with a transparent background, so you can still see your surroundings,    บ
 บ  but this makes it very difficult to see the lines leading from the body   บ
 บ  to the armor column on the right, you have to put body armor in the       บ
 บ  middle slot. Stupid flaws, movement problems, and an annoying delay       บ
 บ  between pushing the map button and actually getting the map (due to it    บ
 บ  changing resolution I think), combine to seriously lower this games       บ
 บ  score, it could've been great.  The movement problems are especially      บ
 บ  pronounced when trying to fight something (combat is realtime), you'll    บ
 บ  die easily.  Get it if you're a rabid rpg fan, if not don't bother.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 58/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SNL Goes Political (c)Berkley Systems [xx.xx]                             บ
 บ  ๚ฤฤฤฤฤฤ . ฤฤ-ฤฤฤ--๚ฤฤ-๚.,y@Q$$"' -ฤฤฤ๚ฤฤ--๚.s                             บ

 บ  ` $'        `                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Disk 11 of this release was badly packaged and had crc errors in      บ
 บ  the arj.  All copies found were like this, but the game still works,      บ
 บ  because the error is in a .mov file and has little effect if any.  This   บ
 บ  rip is basically a total waste of time.  The cd is mainly comprised of    บ
 บ  .mov from various decades in SNL.  There are four games included that     บ
 บ  deal with SNL.  One is where you are that fat dude who looks like Newt    บ
 บ  Gingrich and you sit there slamming bills that come by on your desk as    บ
 บ  fast asa possible.  Another is pacman, but with Bill Clinton and          บ
 บ  hamburgers.  Yet another is a puzzle game, and the last one is a weird    บ
 บ  board type game where you try to get votes by moving the pieces a         บ
 บ  certain way.  It's not worth 22 disks for just those four games.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 42/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  +--------\___/๗e๗/aL!\/--------/_____\-----+           OF LUNATIC         บ
 บ  The Settlers II (English) (c) Blue Byte 1/7                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A word about installation : make sure the path you change in the      บ
 บ  setup.ini points to the s2 subdir, and not the settlers2 dir, else it     บ
 บ  won't work.  I haven't had a long look at this, but it appears to be      บ
 บ  Settlers 1 (also known as Serf City) with nicer graphics, and more        บ
 บ  easily available information.  Everything was represented pictorially in  บ
 บ  the first one, which meant much rereading of the manual to figure out     บ
 บ  what the hell was going on.  The interface is very similar, so anyone     บ
 บ  who's played the 1st one will have no problems getting right into this.   บ
 บ  It apears to support multi-player options, network at least (One          บ
 บ  scenario had 7 players).  Settlers2 supports a variety of resolutions,    บ
 บ  from 640x480 up to 1024x768, and looks very nice.  For people who         บ
 บ  haven't got a clue what it is, Settlers2 is a strategy game where you     บ
 บ  tell your people what to build, where to build it, and provide them with  บ
 บ  roads to get there, presented in a 3/4 sort of view.  Provided you have   บ
 บ  the necessary raw materials, you'll get a little guy who goes out and     บ
 บ  flattens the area, then an engineer comes out and waits for the building  บ
 บ  materials, then people transport the materials to him and you watch as    บ
 บ  he constructs the building.  You have lumberjacks to cut down trees,      บ
 บ  foresters to plant more trees, little guys who quarry stone, miners,      บ
 บ  surveyors (so you know where to build mines), and all sorts of other      บ
 บ  cool shit.  Eventually, you tell your knights to bash the enemy, and      บ
 บ  watch the little guys sword-fighting (very cool), and hopefully bash the  บ
 บ  enemy and take over their territory.  A cool game if u like strategy      บ
 บ  games, and very nicely presented.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 87/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EARTH WORM JIM II - DOS *WORKING* [5/5]                                   บ

 บ  ===============[ ๚D๚O๚G๚S๚ ]================                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well finnaly, a version for all of non-macint...I mean win95 users.   บ
 บ  EWJ2 is everything you could expect it to be based on the first one.      บ
 บ  Totally new ideas, from making sure puppy's land safely across to using   บ
 บ  old grandma's special chair to go up the stairs to picking up cows and    บ

 บ  F. T. B. H. BASEBALL FULL CRACK                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you don't have a joystick, in order to get into the game you need  บ
 บ  to hit your pause/break key like as soon as the jostick calibration menu  บ
 บ  comes up or it will kick your ass into dos.  However as my limited        บ
 บ  explorations into the game have found, you won't be able to play the      บ
 บ  game with the keyboard anyway b/c the keys they have set for it don't     บ
 บ  fucking work!  And of course in all the detailed programming that went    บ
 บ  into this, they couldn't add one more thing so you could make your own    บ
 บ  working keys.  The problem comes when you try to pitch the ball, it       บ
 บ  well, just doesn't pitch.  The k/b keys are just majorly whack.  The      บ
 บ  game however looks great, you have all the fields, all the real players,  บ
 บ  and an excellent game engine that brings back the feeling of good arcade  บ
 บ  like baseball games rather than simulation types.  If only I could        บ
 บ  actually play a full game.  Some other really cool things that happen     บ
 บ  are: (1) The computer doesn't pitch to you, it likes having a starig      บ
 บ  contest w/ the batter I guess (2) When ya hit pause/break for the menu    บ
 บ  in the game and you choose leave game and put it on yes, it just doesn't  บ
 บ  leave, that's pretty cool.  Don't get it unless ya got a joystick.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Top 5 / Bottom 5 DIZs                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I remember back in the days of Legacy when people would always        บ
 บ  complain about our DIZ saying "It's just a generic TheDraw font!!!"       บ
 บ  "Sure," I would respond, "but what's wrong with that!?"  I never managed  บ
 บ  to grasp the reasoning behind spending so much time on a great DIZ.  I    บ
 บ  actually liked our DIZ, it was legible, eye-pleasing, yet didn't go out   บ
 บ  of its way to get your attention.  Nevertheless, people have always had   บ
 บ  a thing for a good DIZ.  So I Rebel Chicken and I decided to go capture   บ
 บ  a bunch of DIZ's and see which we thought were the most extravagantly     บ
 บ  beautiful, and which we thought were the most putridly ugly.  Both Rebel  บ
 บ  and I scored on a scale of 0-5, 0 being "Damn, that's the ugliest thing   บ
 บ  I's ever seen!" and 5 being "Goddamn whatta DIZ!"  We added the scores    บ
 บ  together to make a final score based on a scale of 0-10, 10 being the     บ
 บ  best.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Following are the 10 (5 Best followed by 5 Beastliest) DIZ's out of   บ
 บ  our pile of 42 that we thought were the most Heavenly/Hideous, the most   บ
 บ  Dazzling/Disgusting, the most Gorgeous/Gastly.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I "collect" NFO files, not very serious, but whenever I see an NFO    บ
 บ  file I don't have, I keep it for fun.  This week's topic seemed kinda     บ
 บ  interesting because I have over 120 different NFO files from this year    บ
 บ  only, that's 5 new NFO groups each week, and there are plenty that I've   บ
 บ  missed.  I know some of these groups have merged into others to form a    บ
 บ  new group and so on, but 120 different groups since January 1st is a      บ
 บ  lot.  A lot of these groups are courier groups, most of them just a       บ
 บ  bunch of wannabe couriers who think it's cool to make a group with some   บ
 บ  fancy name.  They have lots of members, and they disappear quick, either  บ
 บ  merged into another group, where the good ones stay and the rest get      บ
 บ  kicked (and probably start another group).                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Then we have the release groups, lots of my NFO's says : "We are a    บ
 บ  new group totally dedicated to releasing quality warez and to have fun,"  บ
 บ  they might release 2-3 things that the "elite" groups wouldn't touch if   บ
 บ  they got paid and then you never hear from'em again, but sometimes they   บ
 บ  have a new supplier that actually does supply quality stuff, but          บ
 บ  he/she(?) probably gets snatched by another group that is a little more   บ
 บ  experienced.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Then we have the groups that come from some local scene, Israel,      บ
 บ  Spain, Finland, Denmark, some area in the US or whatever, that            บ
 บ  unfortunately thinks it's a good idea to go worldwide, they have hardly   บ
 บ  any luck making it big internationally but they do provide something for  บ
 บ  the local scene, pushing warez to the national small 1 node BBSes.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      These "easy come, easy go" groups doesn't do much for the whole       บ
 บ  scene in my view, but they do provide a starting point for the newbie     บ
 บ  who has the talent.  A newbie would never be able to join RiSC or PWA     บ
 บ  first day in the scene so it's a good way for them to prove themselves    บ
 บ  to the scene.   If they're good they'll be noticed and picked up by some  บ
 บ  elite group.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I usually download every piece of software I find, even if it's from  บ
 บ  some unknown group, they deserve a chance, but if I find Quake or         บ
 บ  Windows NT v4.0 released by KRADiCAL iNTERNET RELEASE KRiMiNALZ or        บ
 บ  something, I skip it, but if it sounds genuine I give it a chance.  I     บ
 บ  would never download some "Necrophilias Guide To Cooking v2.1 BETA"       บ
 บ  though, but then I'm not necrophilic either.  It is up to the one that    บ
 บ  finds it to download it, but their releases seldom has mass appeal, it's  บ
 บ  usually some unknown utility/game that not many will benefit from, but    บ
 บ  they don't hurt the scene when releasing, after all it's what the scene   บ
 บ  is about.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Aquistic                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Aquistic,                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, one reason I believe that people start these one week groups    บ
 บ  is, some people have a big thing with taglines, when they enter a room    บ
 บ  they have to have a 40 character tagline to feel important.  They don't   บ
 บ  seem to realize how much work goes into running even a small group and    บ
 บ  actually try to do something with it.  The one week groups don't exactly  บ
 บ  hurt anything, but they don't really help anything.  This morning I had   บ
 บ  someone message me about his 1 day old group and how they did 3 releases  บ
 บ  today alone.  When people say this to me i ask, what have you released    บ
 บ  that was good?  I usually get silence, or am told I am not eleet enough   บ
 บ  to know good from bad.  It is rare for these little groups to release     บ
 บ  something of high quality, BUT it does happen, just not enough :).        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for one week courier groups, WHO THE FUCK ARE YOU GONNA COURIER    บ
 บ  FOR???  All the big groups have had the same couriers for A LONG TIME,    บ
 บ  and there are so many courier groups out now that it doesn't make any     บ
 บ  sense to start another.  If you think you are good enough to make your    บ
 บ  own group run that good, join Motiv8 or Malice, they already have the     บ
 บ  affiliations.  I just watched a new courier group die.  I was told how    บ
 บ  they have these great FTP sites, and all this shit, BUT, there is         บ
 บ  nothing to courier!  Now, I know I will catch shit from some of the       บ
 บ  small groups, BUT, we will wait a month and if you are still around       บ
 บ  good..  If not, well...see ya!                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By the way, I always try to help the small new release groups all I   บ
 บ  can.  They usually have REAL nice members, and are still having fun at    บ
 บ  this.  Some of the older groups' members turn into dicks, and think they  บ
 บ  are all WAY ELEET, and don't have the time to deal with real people.      บ
 บ  Join a new group's channel and it is usually pretty laid back and happy.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Next Week's Topic : Gay Homosexual Elites???                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Next week's topic is not going to be about warez, but rather          บ
 บ  something that is always being made fun of and fought about.  I want      บ
 บ  EVERYONE's opinion about faggots on IRC (yes, I said faggots, I'm not     บ
 บ  politically correct).  The reason I chose this topic is, I have seen      บ
 บ  people become VERY upset if they think someone is gay.  I would just      บ
 บ  like to know what you think about this.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน

 บ      The following details your forecasts depending on your astrological   บ
 บ  sign.  Each sign designates your personal lucky numbers of the week.      บ
 บ  The following specific areas of focus include those of love and warez :   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aquarius> (January 21 to February 19) : A wonderful alignment of the     บ
 บ             Sun and your ruler Uranus suggests that an unforeseen event    บ
 บ             such as constipation will be sure to be within your reach.     บ
 บ             Don't appear to bein too much of a hurry, and drink a lot of   บ
 บ             prune juice.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pisces> (February 20 to March 20): You can't afford to sit on IRC all    บ
 บ           day when your future happiness and security are at risk.         บ
 บ           Indeed, you'd be well advised to make your intentions known.     บ
 บ           If you are gay, or your name so happens to be Incarante, do not  บ
 บ           be afraid to come out of the closet, with Mercury resuming its   บ
 บ           normal direction over the Moon this coming week, this would be   บ
 บ           a perfect time.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aries> (March 21 to April 20) : Don't be put off by someone's lack of    บ
 บ          faith in your abilities to join a warez group.  You ruler Mars,   บ
 บ          strongly supported by Jupiter, is opening the right doors.  All   บ
 บ          you have to do is send some applications to warez groups, and     บ
 บ          you're bound to be accepted with open arms.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Taurus> (April 21 to May 21) : This is not the moment to sacrifice an    บ
 บ           ambition or ignore a professional opportunity.  In fact, you     บ
 บ           could hardly pick a better week to start your very own Internet  บ
 บ           warez group.  However, if you do start an Internet warez group   บ
 บ           this week, don't fool yourself in believing that your group      บ
 บ           will last more than a few days.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Gemini> (May 22 to June 21) : Finish what you start this week, or you    บ
 บ           could end up losing out to someone who lacks your style, talent  บ
 บ           and knowledge.  After your ruler Mercury alters its course to    บ
 บ           the Moon, there will be nothing to stop you from pulling off a   บ
 บ           potentially major coup.  If your name so happens to be Digital   บ
 บ           Vampire, this is a perfect time to name yourself the new leader  บ
 บ           of the dead courier group MALiCE, you are sure to succeed.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Cancer> (June 22 to July 23) : Positive planetary activity in your       บ
 บ           opposing sing of Capricorn suggest that you no longer have to    บ
 บ           toe the line regarding an especially intense Internet            บ
 บ           relationship.  You'll get what you want even sooner than you     บ
 บ           expected.  If your name so happens to be Winterhawk, utilizing   บ
 บ           more than one dildo at a time will satisfy your needs.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Leo> (July 24 to August 23) : Your ruler, the Sun, in conjunction with   บ
 บ        Uranus, planet of the unexpected, suggests that a sudden turn in    บ
 บ        events is about to upstage a partnership issue on a FTP site or on  บ
 บ        a BBS.  Since you're able to turn the tide in your favor, you       บ
 บ        should do so, even if it means upsetting others.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Virgo> (August 24 to September 23) : With your communicative ruler       บ
 บ          Mercury resuming its regular projectory to the Moon, it's time    บ
 บ          for you to plan a change.  Come up with a new handle, and you     บ
 บ          will receive good luck.  There are those who many try to impede   บ
 บ          your progress, but you know more than they do.  The more idiotic  บ
 บ          your new handle, the more you stand to gain.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Libra> (September 24 to October 23) : The combined influence of          บ
 บ          assertive Mars and confident Jupiter will encourage you to        บ
 บ          pursue whatever action it takes regarding your cybersex life.     บ
 บ          There are those who will call you names, ignore their words, and  บ
 บ          you will find true happiness.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Scorpio> (October 24 to November 22) : It's time to show a certain       บ
 บ            person that you're not kidding around, and that you're not      บ
 บ            prepared to stay on the sidelines for a minute longer than      บ
 บ            necessary.  There have been rumblings among the IRC channels    บ
 บ            you frequent, and only you can quiet the situation.             บ

 บ                are in a position to provide tremendous help for someone    บ
 บ                close, it would be churlish not to.                         บ

 ฿ฐ       m a d   r c n !   ฿฿                 ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿
                              ฐ฿฿฿฿฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Chicken-Watch : Part Deux                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I sort of gave up on our Chicken for a few weeks, I figured it was    บ
 บ  hopeless.  I was right.  So I came over to spend the night last night     บ
 บ  because we were going to work on RCN #17.  We also brought Xenon over so  บ
 บ  he could code some stuff for us.  I got in my sleeping bag, we were       บ
 บ  going to talk a bit about the articles for the upcoming issue, talk       บ
 บ  about the cover story, and I noticed something weird happening in he      บ
 บ  bunk above me.  No, he wasn't jacking off, it was worse.  No, he wasn't   บ
 บ  playing footsie with Xenon, it was worse than that too.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Apparently our Chicken has come up with a new habit.  He had a        บ
 บ  puppet of a Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtle Michelangelo in his arms.  I lay  บ
 บ  their, confused for a bit, and proceeded to question him "Ummm, Rebel,    บ
 บ  what the fuck is a ninja turtle doing in your arms?"  He looked at me     บ
 บ  and replied "Um, it's my turtle."  I, still confused, lay there           บ
 บ  wondering what the reason for this awkwardness could be.  A 17-year old   บ
 บ  guy sleeping with a stuffed turtle.  Seemed kinda twisted to me.  So      บ
 บ  after much pondering, I have come to a conclusion as to what the problem  บ
 บ  could be.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      He's still chickless and desperate.  Maybe he thought it would work   บ
 บ  if he replaced the girls with dolls.  I'm running out of options.  I've   บ
 บ  seen some rejects before, I've gotten them out of messes, but this, this  บ
 บ  is like trying to dig a hole to China.  He often reassures me that it     บ
 บ  won't be like this in College (just 2 months away!) and that he'll be     บ
 บ  better then, but I see no way for a guy to ask a girl out in College if   บ
 บ  you've never done it before.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A couple of weeks ago I thought I saw the light at the end of this    บ
 บ  long tunnel.  Some girl asked our Rebel to a 50's dance.  Furthermore,    บ
 บ  it was a girl that he LIKED!  I began to frantically kiss the floor and   บ
 บ  sing halleluyah, but then common sense kicked in and reminded me that he  บ
 บ  didn't necessarily say he would go.  So of course I find out that this    บ
 บ  was his chance of a lifetime and he said no.  What an idiot.  And what's  บ
 บ  worse is that his excuse to me was that he was too busy that night, he    บ
 บ  had to work on RCN.  Judging by the amount of people that message         บ
 บ  RblChickn "have you scored yet?" upon his logging on to IRC, I feel       บ
 บ  comfortable saying that the scene as a whole wouldn't mind RCN a day      บ
 บ  late if the Chicken were to go out on a date.  So now I've completely     บ
 บ  given up on him.  I couldn't get him to go out with a chick when he had   บ
 บ  to be the one to ask, I couldn't when I had to be the one to ask, and I   บ
 บ  can't even when the girl asks.  Rebel, good luck in college, you'll sure  บ
 บ  be needing it ;-).                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
